第一部分 · 宏观全景

01 · LlamaIndex 与 RAG 是什么

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

LlamaIndex 是一个把检索增强生成（RAG）这条数据管道标准化、可编排的框架。它不训练模型，只负责模型周边的全部管道：把你的数据加载、切块、向量化、建索引，再在提问时检索相关片段、喂给 LLM 生成有依据的回答。LlamaIndex is a framework that standardizes and orchestrates the Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipeline. It doesn't train models — it owns everything around them: loading, chunking, embedding and indexing your data, then at query time retrieving the relevant pieces and feeding them to the LLM for a grounded answer.

加载Load
→
切块Split
→
向量化Embed

存储Store

合成Synthesize

回答Answer
RAG 全景：左半是写入路径（建好索引，做一次），右半是查询路径（据此作答，做很多次）The RAG pipeline at a glance: the left half (write path) builds the index once; the right half (query path) answers from it, many times
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
把 LLM 想成一个聪明但在闭卷考试的学生：只能凭记忆答题，记不住就开始编。RAG 让它开卷——先翻到相关页（检索），再据此作答（生成）。LlamaIndex 就是帮你建好这座图书馆和索书系统的工具。
Picture an LLM as a smart student in a closed-book exam: it answers from memory and invents things it can't recall. RAG makes it open-book — find the relevant pages first (retrieve), then answer from them (generate). LlamaIndex builds that library and its call-number system.

RAG 解决什么问题？What problem does RAG solve?

痛点Pain point只用 LLMLLM alone用 RAGWith RAG
知识截止Knowledge cutoff训练后的新知识一概不知Blind to anything after training先检索实时/私有资料再答Retrieves fresh/private data first
幻觉Hallucination不确定也答得很自信Confidently makes things up答案有检索到的出处支撑Answers grounded in retrieved sources
私有数据Private data没见过你的文档Never saw your documents把你的文档建成可检索索引Indexes your docs for retrieval

三个痛点，同一个根因Three pains, one root cause

知识截止、幻觉、私有数据看似三件事，根因只有一个：模型的知识在训练时就被冻结在参数里，既无法更新，也说不清依据。RAG 不去改这套被冻结的参数，而是在提问时临时挂载一份可检索的外部资料，让答案有据可查、随时可换。
Knowledge cutoff, hallucination and private data look like three problems but share one root cause: the model's knowledge is frozen into its weights at training time — it can neither refresh nor cite. RAG doesn't touch those frozen weights; it mounts a searchable external corpus at query time so answers stay grounded and the knowledge stays swappable.
知识更新 / 新文档Knowledge update / new docs
→
重建索引（分钟级）Rebuild the index (minutes)
→
同一个模型零改动Same model, zero changes
→
新答案立即生效New answers take effect at once
RAG 把模型的“记忆”外置成可随时重建的索引——更新知识不必碰模型RAG externalizes the model's memory into a rebuildable index — update knowledge without touching the model
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
llama_index/core/__init__.py · VectorStoreIndex · SimpleDirectoryReader — RAG 的高层入口都从这里导出the high-level RAG entry points are exported here
深入：RAG 的来龙去脉Deep dive: the why and how of RAG点击展开expand
🧪 示例：直接塞进 prompt 会怎样🧪 Example: what if you just stuff the prompt
把整本手册粘进 prompt 看似省事，但会撞上上下文长度上限、推理更慢更贵，且模型容易“迷失在中间”而漏掉关键句。RAG 只挑最相关的几段进 prompt，既省 token 又更准。
Pasting a whole manual into the prompt seems easy, but you hit the context-length ceiling, pay more for slower inference, and the model tends to get “lost in the middle” and miss key lines. RAG feeds only the few most relevant snippets — cheaper and more accurate.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把知识外置成可检索索引，意味着更新知识只需重建索引、模型零改动；同一个模型可服务无数套互不相同的私有库。
Externalizing knowledge into a searchable index means updating knowledge is just rebuilding the index — the model never changes, and one model can serve countless private corpora.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
from_documents 在写入路径里把文档切块、向量化、写进索引；query 在查询路径里把问题向量化、取最近邻、再交给 LLM 据此作答——两行 API 各藏了一条管道。
from_documents runs the write path (split → embed → store); query runs the query path (embed the question → nearest-neighbor search → LLM answers from them) — each one-liner hides a pipeline.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
微调把知识焊进参数（更新贵、难溯源）；超长上下文直接全塞（贵且会“迷失在中间”）；RAG 取两者之间——外置、可更新、可溯源，是私有或时效性知识的默认选择。
Fine-tuning welds knowledge into weights (costly to update, hard to cite); ultra-long context just dumps everything in (expensive, “lost in the middle”); RAG sits in between — external, refreshable, citable — the default for private or time-sensitive knowledge.
最小可运行 RAG：5 行A minimal runnable RAG in 5 lines
pip install llama-index

from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, SimpleDirectoryReader

# 写入路径：加载 -> 切块 -> 向量化 -> 建索引（一行搞定）
docs = SimpleDirectoryReader('./data').load_data()
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)

# 查询路径：检索 -> 合成 -> 有依据的回答
engine = index.as_query_engine()
print(engine.query('这些文档讲了什么？'))
可溯源查询：每个答案都能追到检索片段Traceable query: trace every answer back to its retrieved snippets
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, SimpleDirectoryReader

index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(
    SimpleDirectoryReader('./data').load_data())

engine = index.as_query_engine(similarity_top_k=3)
resp = engine.query('退款要多久到账？')

print(resp)                      # 有依据的回答
for n in resp.source_nodes:      # 答案的出处，可逐条核对
    print(round(n.score, 3), n.node.get_content()[:60])
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • RAG = 先检索相关片段，再让 LLM 据此生成，避免重训与幻觉。RAG = retrieve relevant snippets, then generate from them — no retraining, fewer hallucinations.
  • LlamaIndex 负责 RAG 的数据与编排，不做训练或推理本身。LlamaIndex owns the data + orchestration of RAG, not training or inference.
  • 两条主线贯穿全书：写入路径（建索引）与查询路径（问答）。Two through-lines: the write path (build the index) and the query path (ask).
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
RAG 的精妙在于把模型的“记忆”外置为一个可随时更新、可检索的索引——更新知识只需重建索引，模型本身原封不动。
RAG's elegance: it externalizes the model's “memory” into a searchable index you can refresh anytime — update knowledge by rebuilding the index, never touching the model.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. RAG（检索增强生成）的核心思想是？What is the core idea of RAG?
  1. 换一个更大的模型Switch to a bigger model
  2. 回答前先检索相关外部片段、塞进上下文再生成Retrieve relevant external snippets first, put them in context, then generate
  3. 把全部数据塞进一个超大提示词Stuff all data into one giant prompt
  4. 重新训练模型以记住新知识Retrain the model to memorize new knowledge
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B RAG = 先检索后生成：用检索到的相关片段作为上下文，让模型据此回答，避免重训成本与知识幻觉。RAG retrieves first, then generates: relevant snippets become context so the model answers from them, avoiding retraining cost and hallucination.
2. LlamaIndex 在 RAG 里主要负责什么？What does LlamaIndex mainly provide for RAG?
  1. 把加载→切块→索引→检索→合成这条管道标准化、可编排Standardizing and orchestrating the load→split→index→retrieve→synthesize pipeline
  2. 提供 GPU 推理Providing GPU inference
  3. 训练 embedding 模型Training embedding models
  4. 托管一个向量数据库服务Hosting a vector database service
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：AAnswer: A LlamaIndex 是 RAG 的“数据与编排框架”：统一各阶段接口，底层换 LLM / 向量库 / embedding 都不改主链路。LlamaIndex is the data + orchestration framework for RAG: it unifies each stage so swapping the LLM / vector store / embedding doesn't change the main pipeline.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要给公司 1 万份内部文档做问答助手。为什么选 RAG，而不是直接微调一个模型、或把文档全塞进长上下文？你当初怎么权衡的？上线后又怎么用数据证明这条路是对的？You're building a Q&A assistant over 10,000 internal docs. Why RAG rather than fine-tuning a model or stuffing everything into long context? How did you weigh it — and after launch, how would you prove with data it was the right call?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：RAG 把知识外置成可检索、可更新、可溯源的索引，是“大 / 私有 / 时效 / 要出处”场景的默认解。① 不微调：微调把知识焊进权重，更新一次要重训、贵且难溯源，更适合改风格而非加事实；② 不长上下文全塞：1 万份装不进窗口，贵且会“迷失在中间”；③ 怎么验证：建一组带标准答案的问题，对比 RAG vs 纯 LLM 基线的 Faithfulness（答案是否忠于检索）与命中率，用数字而非感觉下结论。🔑 Key: RAG externalizes knowledge into a searchable, refreshable, citable index — the default for large / private / time-sensitive knowledge that needs sources. (1) Not fine-tuning: it welds knowledge into weights, costly to update and hard to cite — better for style than facts; (2) not long-context dumping: 10k docs don't fit, it's expensive and 'lost in the middle'; (3) validate by comparing RAG vs a plain-LLM baseline on a labeled question set — Faithfulness and hit-rate — concluding from numbers, not vibes.

三条路线的权衡：RAG 在“可更新 + 可溯源 + 规模”上取胜Trade-offs: RAG wins on refreshable + citable + scale
🎯 2. 用户反馈助手“还是会编”。在 RAG 框架下，你会按什么顺序排查？每一步怎么用数据验证而不是猜？Users say the assistant 'still makes things up'. In what order would you investigate, and how would you verify each step with data rather than guess?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：先看 source_nodes，把问题定位到“检索”还是“生成”，再分而治之。① 检索：retrieve() 有没有命中正确依据？没有→召回问题（调 top_k / 换 embedding / 改切块），用命中率量化；② 生成：依据对但答案越界→收紧 prompt（只依据资料、给出处），用 Faithfulness 评估对比改前改后；③ 建一个小回归集，每次改动重测，挡住“修好一个、悄悄弄坏一批”。🔑 Key: look at source_nodes first to localize whether it's retrieval or generation, then divide and conquer. (1) Retrieval: did retrieve() surface the right evidence? If not → recall problem (tune top_k / swap embedding / re-chunk), quantified by hit-rate; (2) generation: right evidence but the answer over-reaches → tighten the prompt (cite-only), compare before/after with a Faithfulness evaluator; (3) keep a small regression set and re-test every change to block 'fix one, silently break many'.
看 source_nodescheck source_nodes
→
检索命中对吗？retrieval right?
否→调召回no → fix recall
→
生成越界吗？generation over-reach?
是→收紧 promptyes → tighten prompt
→
回归集复测re-test on regression set
先定位再修：每一步都用指标验证Localize, then fix — verify each step with a metric

  • 如果你的文档每天都在更新，你会如何设计“增量重新索引”的策略？If your documents change daily, how would you design an incremental re-indexing strategy?
第一部分 · 宏观全景

02 · 架构全景

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

LlamaIndex 分两层：core（稳定的抽象与编排）+ 300+ 集成包（具体的 LLM / Embedding / 向量库实现）。命名约定一眼区分：导入路径带 core 的是核心抽象，不带的是某个第三方集成。LlamaIndex has two layers: core (stable abstractions + orchestration) and 300+ integration packages (concrete LLM / embedding / vector-store implementations). The import path tells them apart: paths with core are core abstractions; those without are a specific third-party integration.

应用 / 你的代码Your app / your code只调用统一抽象，几乎不感知底层换没换calls the unified abstractions, barely notices swaps below
llama-index-corellama-index-core稳定的抽象与编排：Index / Retriever / QueryEngine …stable abstractions + orchestration: Index / Retriever / QueryEngine …
300+ 集成包300+ integration packages各家 LLM / Embedding / 向量库 的具体实现concrete LLM / embedding / vector-store implementations
两层结构：core 定接口、集成填实现，应用只依赖 coreTwo layers: core defines the interfaces, integrations fill them in, and your app depends only on core
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
core 像主板上的标准插槽，集成包像各品牌的内存条/显卡：只要符合插槽规范，插上即用，换品牌不用换主板。
core is the standard slots on a motherboard; integrations are branded RAM/GPUs: anything that fits the slot just works, and swapping brands never means swapping the board.

命名约定：一眼看出是核心还是集成Naming: spot core vs integration at a glance

导入Import含义Meaning
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndexfrom llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex核心抽象（稳定接口）core abstraction (stable interface)
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAIfrom llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAIOpenAI LLM 集成实现the OpenAI LLM integration
from llama_index.embeddings.huggingface import ...from llama_index.embeddings.huggingface import ...HuggingFace Embedding 集成the HuggingFace embedding integration
from llama_index.vector_stores.chroma import ...from llama_index.vector_stores.chroma import ...Chroma 向量库集成the Chroma vector-store integration

为什么把接口和实现拆开Why split interfaces from implementations

core 只定义“能做什么”的抽象接口，具体“怎么做”交给独立集成包。于是新增一个 LLM 或向量库厂商，只需发布一个集成包，core 不必改动、也不必跟着发版；你的应用只依赖 core 的稳定接口，换厂商几乎零成本。
core defines only the abstract “what”; each concrete “how” lives in a separate integration. So adding a new LLM or vector-store vendor is just publishing one integration package — core never changes or re-releases, and because your app depends only on core's stable interface, swapping vendors is near-free.
BaseLLM 接口（core）BaseLLM interface (core)
OpenAIOpenAI
llama-index-llms-openaillama-index-llms-openai
AnthropicAnthropic
llama-index-llms-anthropicllama-index-llms-anthropic
HuggingFaceHuggingFace
llama-index-llms-huggingfacellama-index-llms-huggingface
Ollama（本地）Ollama (local)
llama-index-llms-ollamallama-index-llms-ollama
一个 core 接口，多份集成实现：插上即用、按需安装One core interface, many integration impls: plug in à la carte
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
llama_index/core/__init__.py · (package root) — core 导出所有稳定抽象；集成包各自独立发版core exports the stable abstractions; integrations ship as separate packages
深入：分层架构的取舍Deep dive: the trade-offs of the layered architecture点击展开expand
🧪 示例：一次装三个包🧪 Example: installing three packages
一个典型项目会装 llama-index-core + llama-index-llms-openai + llama-index-embeddings-openai：核心一份，其余按需各取所需。
A typical project installs llama-index-core + llama-index-llms-openai + llama-index-embeddings-openai: one core, the rest à la carte.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
让生态可独立演进：300+ 厂商各自迭代发版，不被 core 的节奏绑死，也不会把彼此的依赖互相拖进来。
It lets the ecosystem evolve independently: 300+ vendors iterate and release on their own cadence, unshackled from core's schedule and from each other's dependencies.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
命名空间约定是关键：llama_index.core.* 是抽象，llama_index.llms.x / llama_index.vector_stores.y 是实现，导入路径一眼可辨。
The namespace convention is the key: llama_index.core.* is abstractions, while llama_index.llms.x / llama_index.vector_stores.y are implementations — the import path tells you which at a glance.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
单体框架（所有实现塞进一个包）安装简单，但依赖臃肿、升级互相牵制；插件式分层用多装几个小包，换来灵活与可维护。
A monolith (all implementations in one package) is simpler to install but bloats dependencies and couples upgrades; the plugin-style split trades a few extra small installs for flexibility and maintainability.
core 定接口，集成填实现core defines interfaces, integrations fill them in
# 核心 + 按需安装集成（每个集成是独立的 pip 包）
pip install llama-index-core
pip install llama-index-llms-openai llama-index-embeddings-openai

from llama_index.core import Settings           # 核心：全局配置
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAI       # 集成：换成别家只改这一行
from llama_index.embeddings.openai import OpenAIEmbedding

Settings.llm = OpenAI(model='gpt-4o-mini')
Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(model='text-embedding-3-small')
换 provider 只改一行：core 之上的代码完全不变Swap provider in one line: everything above core stays the same
# 同一套链路，换一家 LLM 只动这一块
from llama_index.core import Settings

# A) OpenAI
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAI
Settings.llm = OpenAI(model='gpt-4o-mini')

# B) 换成 Anthropic：只改导入 + 这一行，其余代码原封不动
from llama_index.llms.anthropic import Anthropic
Settings.llm = Anthropic(model='claude-3-5-sonnet-latest')
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 导入路径带 core = 核心抽象；不带 = 第三方集成实现。Import path with core = core abstraction; without = a third-party integration.
  • 集成是独立 pip 包，按需安装，互不绑定版本。Integrations are separate pip packages, installed à la carte.
  • 换 LLM 只改一行；换 Embedding 还得重建索引（向量要重算）；换向量库改的是存储注入——三者代价不同。Swapping the LLM is a one-liner; swapping the embedding also forces a re-index (vectors must be recomputed); swapping the vector store changes storage wiring — different costs.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
这套分层的真正红利：本地用 Ollama 把整条 RAG 跑通，上线只把 Settings.llm 换成 OpenAI——retriever / index / query engine 一行都不用改。
The real dividend of this layering: prototype the whole RAG locally on Ollama, then ship by swapping just Settings.llm to OpenAI — your retriever / index / query engine don't change a line.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 看到 from llama_index.vector_stores.chroma import ...，你能立刻判断什么？Seeing from llama_index.vector_stores.chroma import ..., what do you instantly know?
  1. 这是一个第三方集成实现（路径不含 core）It's a third-party integration (path has no core)
  2. Chroma 是 LlamaIndex 官方维护的Chroma is maintained by LlamaIndex itself
  3. 这是 core 的稳定抽象It's a stable core abstraction
  4. 必须先 import core 才能用它You must import core before it works
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：AAnswer: A 命名约定：路径不含 core 即为具体集成实现；core 只定义接口。By convention, a path without core is a concrete integration; core only defines interfaces.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要给团队定规范：什么时候用现成集成包、什么时候自己封装。core/集成分层怎么帮你做这个决定？你又怎么验证“换厂商真的低成本”？You're setting a team rule: when to use an off-the-shelf integration vs roll your own. How does the core/integration split inform that, and how would you verify that 'swapping vendors is really cheap'?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：路径含 core=抽象，不含=集成实现；优先用现成集成，只有专有需求才自封装。现成集成久经测试、独立发版；自写要实现 core 的接口。验证：写一个“换 LLM 只改 Settings.llm 一行”的冒烟测试，跑同一组问题看链路不崩——但注意换 Embedding 要重建索引，那一项并非零成本。🔑 Key: a path with core = abstraction, without = integration; prefer existing integrations, roll your own only for proprietary needs. Existing ones are battle-tested and ship independently; custom ones implement the core interface. Verify with a smoke test that swaps the LLM via one Settings.llm line and re-runs a question set — but note swapping the embedding forces a re-index, which isn't free.
🎯 2. 本地用 Ollama 跑通的 RAG 要上线换 OpenAI。你的迁移清单是什么？哪一步最容易出事，怎么提前验证？A local Ollama RAG goes live on OpenAI. What's your migration checklist, which step is most dangerous, and how do you de-risk it ahead of time?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：换 LLM 是一行；最容易出事的是换 Embedding——必须重建索引。迁移清单：改 Settings.llm；retriever / index / query engine 不动；若也换 embedding，则在 staging 用新模型重建一遍索引、跑回归集对比分数，确认召回没退化再切流量——直接热切会让旧向量与新查询坐标系不可比。🔑 Key: swapping the LLM is one line; the dangerous step is swapping the embedding — it forces a re-index. Checklist: change Settings.llm; leave retriever / index / query engine; if the embedding also changes, rebuild the index with the new model in staging and compare a regression set before shifting traffic — a hot swap leaves old vectors incomparable to new queries.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 把接口放在 core、实现放在集成包，这种分层在什么情况下反而会成为负担？Putting interfaces in core and implementations in integrations — when might this layering become a burden rather than a benefit?
第一部分 · 宏观全景

03 · 一次 RAG 的生命周期

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

那 5 行代码背后是两个阶段：写入路径（建索引，做一次）和查询路径（问答，做很多次）。高层 API 把每个阶段的细节藏了起来——本课先看全景，后面逐站拆解。Those 5 lines hide two phases: the write path (build the index, once) and the query path (ask, many times). The high-level API hides each stage's detail — this lesson is the map; later lessons visit each stop.

SimpleDirectoryReader(...).load_data()SimpleDirectoryReader(...).load_data()→ Document 列表→ a list of Document
↓
VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)→ Node → 向量 → 写入索引（切块见第 6 课 · 向量化见第 8 课）→ Node → vectors → stored in the index (split → L6 · embed → L8)
↓
index.as_query_engine()index.as_query_engine()→ 装配 检索 / 后处理 / 合成→ wires retrieve / post-process / synthesize
↓
engine.query('…')engine.query('…')→ 检索 → 合成 → 答案 + source_nodes（检索见第 12 课 · 合成见第 14 课）→ retrieve → synthesize → answer + source_nodes (retrieve → L12 · synthesize → L14)
四行 API，每一行的产出正好喂给下一行Four API lines — each line's output is exactly the next line's input
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
写入路径像建图书馆：收书、拆章节、编索书号、上架。查询路径像借阅问答：按主题找到相关几页，读完再用自己的话回答你。
The write path is like building a library: collect books, split chapters, assign call numbers, shelve. The query path is like asking the librarian: find the few relevant pages, read them, answer in their own words.

把 5 行代码映射到流水线Mapping the 5 lines onto the pipeline

代码Code阶段Stage幕后发生了什么What happens under the hood
SimpleDirectoryReader(...).load_data()SimpleDirectoryReader(...).load_data()加载Load文件 → Document 列表files → list of Document
VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)切块+向量化+索引Split + embed + indexDocument → Node → 向量 → 存入索引Document → Node → vectors → stored in the index
index.as_query_engine()index.as_query_engine()装配查询Assemble query检索器 + 后处理 + 响应合成器 组装好wires retriever + postprocessors + synthesizer

高层 API 只是低层管道的快捷方式The high-level API is just a shortcut over the low-level pipeline

那几行高层 API 并没有发明新东西，它们只是把底层管道的默认装配“一键化”。新手用一行跑通，进阶者可以拆开任意一站、替换其中的组件——同一套抽象，支持两种使用深度。
Those few high-level lines invent nothing new; they merely package the low-level pipeline's default wiring into one click. Beginners get it running in a line; experts open any stop and swap its components — one set of abstractions, two depths of use.
写入路径（做一次）Write path (run once)
加载 → 切块 → 向量化 → 建索引。较重但只需一次，产物是可复用的索引。
Load → split → embed → index. Heavier, but one-off; the product is a reusable index.
vs
查询路径（做很多次）Query path (run many times)
检索 → 后处理 → 合成。每次提问都走一遍，复用同一个索引，秒级返回。
Retrieve → post-process → synthesize. Runs on every question, reusing the same index, in seconds.
建一次索引，问无数次Build the index once, query it countless times
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
indices/base.py · BaseIndex.from_documents — 写入路径的“快捷方式”（VectorStoreIndex 继承自 BaseIndex），内部串起 split→embed→storethe write-path shortcut (VectorStoreIndex inherits it from BaseIndex); chains split→embed→store inside
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
base/base_query_engine.py · BaseQueryEngine.query — 查询路径的统一入口the unified entry point of the query path
深入：两行 API 各藏了什么Deep dive: what the two one-liners hide点击展开expand
🧪 示例：还是那 5 行🧪 Example: those same 5 lines
load_data → from_documents → as_query_engine → query 四步，就是一个完整 RAG 的最短写法；本书后面每一课，都是在拆开其中的某一步。
load_data → from_documents → as_query_engine → query is the shortest complete RAG; every later lesson in this guide simply opens up one of those steps.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
快捷方式降低上手门槛，又不牺牲可定制性：默认装配开箱即用，需要时再逐站替换，二者共用同一套对象。
Shortcuts lower the barrier to entry without sacrificing customizability: the default wiring works out of the box, and you can replace any stop when needed — both share the very same objects.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
from_documents 内部依次跑 split → embed → store，把 Document 变成带向量的 Node 存进索引；query 内部跑 retrieve → synthesize，把问题变成答案。
from_documents internally runs split → embed → store, turning Documents into vector-bearing Nodes in the index; query internally runs retrieve → synthesize, turning a question into an answer.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
你完全可以手动逐站装配（自建 node_parser / embed_model / retriever / synthesizer），换取最大控制力；高层 API 只是把这套装配的常见默认值替你填好。
You can always wire each stop by hand (your own node_parser / embed_model / retriever / synthesizer) for maximum control; the high-level API just fills in that wiring's common defaults for you.
同一个 index，写一次、问多次one index: write once, query many times
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, SimpleDirectoryReader

# —— 写入路径（建一次索引）——
docs = SimpleDirectoryReader('./data').load_data()   # 加载
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)        # 切块+向量化+索引

# —— 查询路径（可反复问）——
engine = index.as_query_engine(similarity_top_k=3)   # 装配
resp = engine.query('退款政策是什么？')              # 检索→合成→回答
print(resp)                  # 答案
print(resp.source_nodes)     # 依据：检索到的片段
把“写一次”落盘，之后秒级复用Persist the “write once” to disk, then reuse it in seconds
from llama_index.core import (
    VectorStoreIndex, SimpleDirectoryReader, StorageContext, load_index_from_storage)

# —— 首次：建好索引并落盘 ——
docs = SimpleDirectoryReader('./data').load_data()
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)
index.storage_context.persist('./storage')

# —— 以后：直接从磁盘加载，跳过重新建索引 ——
ctx = StorageContext.from_defaults(persist_dir='./storage')
index = load_index_from_storage(ctx)
engine = index.as_query_engine()
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 写入路径做一次、查询路径做多次；二者共享同一个 index。Write path runs once, query path many times; both share one index.
  • from_documents 隐藏了 split→embed→store；as_query_engine 隐藏了 retrieve→synthesize。from_documents hides split→embed→store; as_query_engine hides retrieve→synthesize.
  • response.source_nodes 让答案可溯源。response.source_nodes makes every answer traceable.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
高层 API 是低层管道的“快捷方式”：新手用一行跑通，进阶者拆开每一站替换组件——同一套抽象，两种使用深度。
The high-level API is a shortcut over the low-level pipeline: beginners get it running in one line; experts open each stop to swap components — one set of abstractions, two depths of use.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs) 一行其实做了哪些事？What does the single line VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs) actually do?
  1. 只是把文档存成文件Just saves the documents to disk
  2. 立刻向 LLM 提问Immediately queries the LLM
  3. 切块 → 向量化 → 存入索引（写入路径三步合一）Split → embed → store (three write-path steps in one)
  4. 训练一个新的 embedding 模型Trains a new embedding model
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 它是写入路径的快捷方式：内部依次切块、调用 embed_model 向量化、写入向量索引。It's the write-path shortcut: internally it chunks, embeds via embed_model, and writes vectors into the index.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要把这套 5 行 demo 变成能扛 1000 QPS 的服务。写入路径和查询路径分别部署在哪？为什么不能每次提问都 from_documents？你怎么验证扩容方案？You're turning the 5-line demo into a 1000-QPS service. Where does each of the write path and query path run, why can't you call from_documents per question, and how do you validate the scaling plan?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：写入路径离线做一次并落盘，查询路径在线、无状态、复用索引。每次提问都 from_documents 等于把 O(语料) 的切块+向量化塞进每个请求——又慢又烧钱、还没法水平扩展。做法：建索引放批处理/后台任务，persist 后查询侧只 load + query。验证：压测查询 QPS / p95 延迟，并确认建索引不在请求热路径上。🔑 Key: the write path runs once offline and is persisted; the query path is online, stateless, and reuses the index. Calling from_documents per question forces O(corpus) split+embed into every request — slow, costly, unscalable. Build in a batch/background job, persist, then the query side only loads + querys. Validate by load-testing query QPS / p95 latency and confirming indexing is off the hot path.
写入路径（做一次）Write path (once)
加载→切块→向量化→建索引→persist；重，离线/批处理。load→split→embed→index→persist; heavy, offline/batch.
vs
查询路径（做很多次）Query path (many times)
load→检索→后处理→合成；轻，在线、无状态、可水平扩展。load→retrieve→post-process→synthesize; light, online, stateless, scales out.
把“建一次”和“问多次”分开部署，才能各自扩容Deploy 'build once' and 'ask many' separately so each scales on its own
🎯 2. 高层 API 把细节藏了起来。你怎么判断“什么时候该拆开用低层 from_args”？举一个必须下沉的例子。The high-level API hides the details. How do you decide when to drop to low-level from_args? Give an example that forces it.
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：默认装配够用就用高层；要替换/插入某一站就下沉到 from_args。二者产出同一种对象、共享同一套抽象，只是装配深度不同。必须下沉的例子：要做“句窗检索 + 相似度过滤 + rerank + 自定义 text_qa_template”的客服引擎——默认 as_query_engine 装不出来，得用 from_args 逐件装。🔑 Key: use the high-level API when default wiring suffices; drop to from_args to replace/insert a stop. Both yield the same object and share the abstractions, differing only in wiring depth. Forcing example: a support engine with sentence-window retrieval + similarity cutoff + rerank + a custom text_qa_template — the default as_query_engine can't assemble that, so you wire it with from_args.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 如果同一个索引要服务上千次提问，你会把哪一步的结果缓存或持久化？为什么？If one index serves thousands of queries, which step's output would you cache or persist, and why?
第二部分 · 写入路径

04 · Document 与 Node 数据模型

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

RAG 的最小检索单位是 Node，不是整篇 Document。Document 是一整份原始资料；切块后得到带元数据与关系的 Node——检索、返回、合成都围绕 Node 进行。The unit of retrieval in RAG is the Node, not the whole Document. A Document is one raw source; chunking yields Nodes carrying metadata and relationships — retrieval, results and synthesis all revolve around Nodes.

NodeNode
text 文本text
用于 embedding 的正文内容the body content that gets embedded
metadata 元数据metadata
键值对，可用于过滤与溯源key-value pairs, usable for filtering and provenance
relationships 关系relationships
SOURCE · PREVIOUS · NEXT，把 Node 串成链SOURCE · PREVIOUS · NEXT, chaining Nodes together
一个 Node = 文本 + 元数据 + 关系，三者一起流经整条管道One Node = text + metadata + relationships, flowing together through the whole pipeline
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
Document 是整本书；Node 是书里的一页便利贴，背面记着“来自哪本书、上一页/下一页是谁”（relationships）和“章节/页码”（metadata）。
A Document is the whole book; a Node is one sticky note from it, whose back records “which book, previous/next note” (relationships) and “chapter/page” (metadata).

Document vs NodeDocument vs Node

DocumentDocumentNode (TextNode)Node (TextNode)
粒度Granularity整份原始资料one whole source切块后的片段a chunked piece
角色Role输入：被切块input: gets chunked检索/合成的单位unit of retrieval/synthesis
携带Carriestext + metadatatext + metadatatext + metadata + relationshipstext + metadata + relationships

为什么以 Node 为检索单位Why the Node is the unit of retrieval

检索、排序、返回、合成全部以 Node 为单位，是为了让下游组件“说同一种语言”：向量库存的是 Node、检索器返回的是 Node、合成器读的也是 Node，无论原始来源是 PDF、网页还是数据库。Document 太粗——一篇上万字里真正相关的常常只有一两段，整篇压成一个向量时，相关内容会被大量无关文字稀释，命中既不准也不稳；Node 把粒度收敛到“一次讲清一件事”的片段，既适配 embedding 的长度上限，又让命中更准、引用更细。
Retrieval, ranking, results and synthesis all operate on Nodes so that every downstream component “speaks one language”: the vector store holds Nodes, the retriever returns Nodes, the synthesizer reads Nodes — whatever the original source. A Document is too coarse — in a 10k-word file usually only a paragraph or two is relevant, and squeezing the whole thing into one vector dilutes that signal with unrelated text, so hits are neither precise nor stable; a Node narrows granularity to “one idea at a time”, fitting the embedding's length limit while making hits sharper and citations finer.
DocumentDocument
一整份原始资料one whole source
→
切块 splitsplit
按 chunk_size 拆分split by chunk_size
→
NodeNode
片段 + 元数据chunk + metadata
→
NodeNode
PREVIOUS ↔ NEXT 相连linked PREVIOUS ↔ NEXT
→
NodeNode
SOURCE 指回 DocumentSOURCE points back to the Document
一份 Document 切成多个 Node；relationships 让它们彼此相连、并各自指回来源One Document becomes many Nodes; relationships link them to one another and back to the source
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
schema.py · Document · TextNode · NodeRelationship · RelatedNodeInfo — 数据模型与节点关系都定义在这里the data model and node relationships live here
深入：Node 作为检索单位Deep dive: the Node as the unit of retrieval点击展开expand
🧪 示例：构造 Node 并连上关系🧪 Example: build a Node and wire its relationships
手动建两个 TextNode，把第二个的 SOURCE 指回 Document、PREVIOUS 指向第一个，就得到一条可前后扩展、可溯源的链：检索命中某个 Node 后，能顺着 NEXT 取下一段补全上下文。
Create two TextNodes by hand, point the second's SOURCE back to the Document and its PREVIOUS to the first, and you get a chain you can expand and trace: after a Node is hit you can follow NEXT to pull the next chunk for fuller context.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把“检索/溯源的单位”固定为 Node，整条管道就只需理解一种对象。粒度统一后，过滤、排序、引用、前后文扩展都有了共同的承载体，组件之间也能自由替换而不必翻译彼此的数据结构。
Fixing the Node as the unit of retrieval and provenance means the whole pipeline only ever reasons about one kind of object. With uniform granularity, filtering, ranking, citation and context expansion share one carrier, and components stay swappable without translating each other's data.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
关系存在 node.relationships 字典里，键是 NodeRelationship 枚举（SOURCE / PREVIOUS / NEXT / PARENT / CHILD），值是 RelatedNodeInfo；node.ref_doc_id 就是顺着 SOURCE 找到的来源文档 id。
Relationships live in the node.relationships dict, keyed by the NodeRelationship enum (SOURCE / PREVIOUS / NEXT / PARENT / CHILD) with RelatedNodeInfo values; node.ref_doc_id is simply the source document id reached via SOURCE.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
直接拿整篇 Document 去检索看似省事，却粒度太粗：长文里相关的只有一两段，整篇的向量被无关内容稀释，命中不准、还浪费上下文。以 Node 为单位，才能既命中精准、又能按需向前后扩展。
Retrieving whole Documents looks simpler but is too coarse: only a paragraph or two is relevant, the whole-doc vector gets diluted by unrelated text, hits are imprecise and context is wasted. Working per Node is what makes hits precise while still allowing on-demand prev/next expansion.
元数据与关系随 Node 一起流动metadata and relationships travel with the Node
from llama_index.core import Document
from llama_index.core.schema import TextNode, NodeRelationship, RelatedNodeInfo

doc = Document(text='LlamaIndex 让 RAG 更简单。', metadata={'source': 'faq.md'})

n1 = TextNode(text='第一段', metadata={'page': 1})
n2 = TextNode(text='第二段', metadata={'page': 2})
# 关系：n2 来自 doc，且紧跟在 n1 之后
n2.relationships[NodeRelationship.SOURCE] = RelatedNodeInfo(node_id=doc.doc_id)
n2.relationships[NodeRelationship.PREVIOUS] = RelatedNodeInfo(node_id=n1.node_id)
print(n2.metadata, n2.relationships.keys())
用 metadata 过滤检索，用 relationships 溯源filter retrieval by metadata, trace provenance via relationships
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex
from llama_index.core.schema import NodeRelationship
from llama_index.core.vector_stores import MetadataFilters, MetadataFilter

index = VectorStoreIndex(nodes)

# 只在 metadata['page'] == 2 的 Node 里检索（元数据过滤）
flt = MetadataFilters(filters=[MetadataFilter(key='page', value=2)])
engine = index.as_query_engine(filters=flt)
print(engine.query('第二页讲了什么？'))

# 顺着 SOURCE 关系溯源：命中的 Node 来自哪个 Document
src = nodes[1].relationships.get(NodeRelationship.SOURCE)
print(src.node_id if src else None)
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Node 是检索单位；Document 只是它的来源。The Node is the unit of retrieval; the Document is just its source.
  • metadata 随 Node 流动，可用于过滤与溯源。metadata flows with the Node, enabling filtering and provenance.
  • relationships（SOURCE/PREVIOUS/NEXT）是进阶检索（如前后文扩展、溯源）的基础。relationships (SOURCE/PREVIOUS/NEXT) underpin advanced retrieval (e.g. prev/next context expansion, provenance).
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
统一的 Node 抽象让整条管道“说同一种语言”：无论来源是 PDF 还是数据库，下游都只面对带元数据与关系的 Node。
A single Node abstraction makes the whole pipeline speak one language: whether the source is a PDF or a database, everything downstream only deals with metadata-and-relationship-bearing Nodes.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. RAG 中真正被检索、并喂给 LLM 的最小单位是？In RAG, what is the smallest unit that actually gets retrieved and fed to the LLM?
  1. 向量本身the vector itself
  2. 原始文件the raw file
  3. 整篇 Documentthe whole Document
  4. Node（切块后带元数据的片段）a Node (a chunked, metadata-bearing piece)
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：DAnswer: D Document 会被切成 Node；检索、返回的 source_nodes、以及响应合成都以 Node 为单位。A Document is split into Nodes; retrieval, the returned source_nodes, and synthesis all operate on Nodes.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要做一个能“精确引用到第几页第几段”的合同问答。为什么检索单位用 Node 而不是整篇 Document？你会怎么设计 Node 的 metadata 与 relationships？怎么验证引用准确？You're building contract Q&A that must cite the exact page and paragraph. Why retrieve Nodes, not whole Documents? How would you design the Node metadata and relationships, and how do you verify citation accuracy?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：Node 让检索精准且可溯源；整篇 Document 的向量会被无关内容稀释、还没法定位。设计：metadata 存 page / section / contract_id 供过滤与溯源，relationships（PREVIOUS/NEXT）串前后文做上下文扩展。验证：抽一批问题，人工核对引用的 page/段落是否真的包含答案，统计引用准确率，而不是只看答案读起来对不对。🔑 Key: Nodes make retrieval precise and citable; a whole-Document vector is diluted by irrelevant text and can't localize. Design: metadata holds page / section / contract_id for filtering and provenance; relationships (PREVIOUS/NEXT) chain neighbors for context expansion. Verify by manually checking, on a sample, whether the cited page/paragraph actually contains the answer — a citation-accuracy rate, not just whether the prose reads right.
🎯 2. 检索老返回“相关但不对”的段落——查 2024 年退款却返回 2022 年的条款。你会怎么用 Node 的 metadata 解决？Retrieval keeps returning related-but-wrong chunks — asking about 2024 refunds returns the 2022 clause. How would you use Node metadata to fix it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：把年份/版本写进 metadata，用 MetadataFilters 先过滤、再语义排序（检索第二通道）。纯向量只懂语义、不懂“限定 2024”这种结构化约束。前提是建索引时就把这些字段抽进每个 Node 的 metadata；否则过滤无从谈起。🔑 Key: put year/version into metadata and use MetadataFilters to filter first, then rank semantically (retrieval's second channel). Pure vectors capture meaning but not structured constraints like 'restrict to 2024'. It works only if those fields were extracted into each Node's metadata at index time.

第二部分 · 写入路径

05 · 数据加载 Readers

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

Reader 把任意来源（文件夹、PDF、网页、数据库……）统一变成 Document 列表。SimpleDirectoryReader 是最常用的入口，按扩展名自动选解析器。A Reader turns any source (a folder, PDF, web page, database…) into a list of Documents. SimpleDirectoryReader is the go-to entry point, picking a parser per file extension.

多来源Many sources
文件夹 · PDF · 网页 · 数据库folder · PDF · web · DB
→
ReaderReader
按来源选解析器pick a parser per source
→
Document 列表List of Documents
统一结构，下游通用one structure, used by everything downstream
千奇百怪的来源，经 Reader 收敛成同一种 DocumentWildly different sources, collapsed by a Reader into one Document type
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
Reader 像一排不同接口的扫描仪：无论纸张、幻灯片还是网页，扫出来都是同一种标准的 Document。
Readers are like a row of scanners with different ports: paper, slides or web pages all come out as the same standard Document.

SimpleDirectoryReader 常用能力What SimpleDirectoryReader gives you

参数Argument作用Effect
input_dir / input_filesinput_dir / input_files读整个目录或指定文件read a folder or specific files
recursive=Truerecursive=True递归子目录recurse subfolders
required_exts=['.pdf']required_exts=['.pdf']只读特定扩展名limit to extensions

一个文件可能产出多个 DocumentOne file can yield many Documents

容易以为“读 N 个文件就得到 N 个 Document”，其实不一定：很多解析器按自然边界切分，一个 PDF 通常每页一个 Document，于是 len(docs) 往往大于文件数。这个粒度会一路向下传导——Document 越多，切出的 Node 越多；而每个 Document 自带的 page_label 等元数据，正是日后“引用到第几页”溯源的依据。所以加载完先 print(len(docs))、看一眼 docs[0].metadata，对后面的切块数量与引用粒度都心里有数。
It's tempting to assume “N files in, N Documents out”, but not necessarily: many parsers split on natural boundaries — a PDF usually yields one Document per page — so len(docs) is often larger than the file count. That granularity propagates downstream: more Documents means more Nodes after chunking, and the page_label each Document carries is exactly what later lets you cite “which page”. So after loading, print(len(docs)) and peek at docs[0].metadata — it tells you a lot about downstream chunk counts and citation granularity.
report.pdf（1 个文件）report.pdf (1 file)
Document(page=1)Document(page=1)
第 1 页正文 + page_labelpage 1's text + page_label
Document(page=2)Document(page=2)
第 2 页正文 + page_labelpage 2's text + page_label
Document(page=3) …Document(page=3) …
逐页扇出，依此类推fanned out page by page, and so on
一个文件按页扇出多个 Document：所以 len(docs) ≠ 文件数，且每个 Document 自带页码供日后溯源One file fans out into many Documents by page — so len(docs) ≠ the file count, and each Document carries its page number for later provenance

readers/file/base.py · SimpleDirectoryReader — 内置目录读取器the built-in directory reader
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
readers/base.py · BaseReader.load_data — 所有 Reader 的统一接口the interface every Reader implements
深入：Reader 与统一 DocumentDeep dive: Readers and the unified Document点击展开expand
🧪 示例：递归读目录、只取特定扩展名🧪 Example: recurse a folder, keep only some extensions
SimpleDirectoryReader(input_dir='./data', recursive=True, required_exts=['.md', '.pdf']) 会递归扫描子目录、只读 .md 与 .pdf，并按扩展名分别用平文本与 PDF 解析器，最后统一产出 Document。
SimpleDirectoryReader(input_dir='./data', recursive=True, required_exts=['.md', '.pdf']) recurses subfolders, keeps only .md and .pdf, parses each with the plain-text or PDF parser by extension, and emits Documents uniformly.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把来源解析与下游处理解耦：管道只认 Document，不关心它来自文件、网页还是数据库。换数据源是“换一个 Reader”，主链路一行不改。
It decouples source parsing from downstream processing: the pipeline only knows Documents, not whether they came from a file, a web page or a database. Changing sources means “swap a Reader” — the pipeline stays untouched.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
SimpleDirectoryReader 内部维护一张扩展名→解析器类的映射（default_file_reader_cls）：遍历文件时按后缀查表、实例化对应解析器、调用其 load_data，把结果汇成一个 Document 列表。
Inside, SimpleDirectoryReader keeps an extension→parser-class map (default_file_reader_cls): it walks files, looks up the suffix, instantiates the matching parser, calls its load_data, and gathers everything into one list of Documents.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
内置解析器覆盖常见文件；更多来源（网页、Notion、Slack、数据库、Google Drive……）在 LlamaHub 上以独立集成包提供，pip install 后即插即用，产出同样是 Document。
Built-in parsers cover common files; more sources (web, Notion, Slack, databases, Google Drive…) live on LlamaHub as separate integration packages — pip install and plug in, still emitting Documents.
一行加载整个目录load a whole directory in one line
from llama_index.core import SimpleDirectoryReader

docs = SimpleDirectoryReader(
    input_dir='./data', recursive=True, required_exts=['.md', '.pdf'],
).load_data()
print(len(docs), docs[0].metadata)   # 每个文件 -> 一个或多个 Document

# 更多来源见 LlamaHub：pip install llama-index-readers-web 等
# from llama_index.readers.web import SimpleWebPageReader
LlamaHub：一个网页也是一份 DocumentLlamaHub: a web page is a Document too
# pip install llama-index-readers-web
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex
from llama_index.readers.web import SimpleWebPageReader

docs = SimpleWebPageReader(html_to_text=True).load_data(
    ['https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/'])
print(len(docs), docs[0].text[:80])

# 网页同样产出 Document —— 与本地文件走完全一样的下游管道
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Reader 的统一产出是 Document，让管道与数据来源解耦。Readers all output Documents, decoupling the pipeline from data sources.
  • SimpleDirectoryReader 按扩展名自动选解析器。SimpleDirectoryReader auto-selects a parser by extension.
  • 更多来源在 LlamaHub（独立集成包，按需安装）。More sources live on LlamaHub (separate integration packages).
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把“千奇百怪的来源”收敛到“一种 Document”，是 RAG 可组合性的起点——换数据源不影响后续任何一站。
Collapsing wildly different sources into one Document type is where RAG composability begins — changing the source never disturbs any later stage.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你的数据来自 PDF、网页、Confluence 三种源，还会不断加新源。你怎么设计加载层让“加新源不影响后面任何一站”？一个 PDF 常常每页一个 Document，这对你估成本和做引用有什么影响？Your data comes from PDFs, web pages and Confluence, with more sources coming. 🎯 2. 自己写一个 Reader vs 用 LlamaHub 现成集成，你怎么定？什么时候自写更划算？Writing your own Reader vs using a LlamaHub integration — how do you decide, and when is rolling your own worth it?

Existing ones are tested and quick; a custom one just implements BaseReader.load_data to return Documents and plugs straight in. The trade-off is maintenance vs control — don't reinvent a wheel for a one-off CSV.

第二部分 · 写入路径

06 · 切块 Node Parsers

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

切块（chunking）把 Document 拆成大小合适的 Node。为什么要切？因为 embedding 与 LLM 上下文都有限，且检索希望命中精准的小片段。chunk_size 与 chunk_overlap 是核心旋钮。Chunking splits a Document into right-sized Nodes. Why split? Because embeddings and LLM context are limited, and retrieval wants to hit a precise small piece. chunk_size and chunk_overlap are the key knobs.

无重叠 chunk_overlap=0No overlap (chunk_overlap=0)
块 A 结尾是“……退款将在 7 个工作”，块 B 开头是“日内原路退回……”——一句话被从中间切断，两个块单独看都答不全。
Chunk A ends with “…refunds arrive within 7 business” and Chunk B starts with “days, to the original method…” — one sentence cut in half; neither chunk answers fully on its own.
vs
有重叠 chunk_overlap=50With overlap (chunk_overlap=50)
块 A 末尾与块 B 开头共享几句，“7 个工作日内原路退回”完整落在某一个块里——检索命中即拿到完整语义。
Chunk A's tail and Chunk B's head share a few sentences, so “within 7 business days to the original method” lands intact in one chunk — hit it and you get the whole thought.
chunk_overlap 让相邻块共享边界句，避免把一句话从中间切断chunk_overlap makes adjacent chunks share boundary sentences, so a thought isn't cut in half
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
把长文拆成便利贴：太大塞不下又检索不准，太小丢上下文。overlap 让相邻便利贴重叠几句，避免把一句话从中间切断。
Cut long text into sticky notes: too big won't fit and retrieves imprecisely; too small loses context. overlap lets adjacent notes share a few sentences so a thought isn't cut mid-way.

四种常用切块器Four common splitters

切块器Splitter切法How it splits适合Good for
SentenceSplitterSentenceSplitter按句子凑到 chunk_sizesentences up to chunk_size通用默认general default
TokenTextSplitterTokenTextSplitter按 token 数硬切by token count严格控长strict length control
SemanticSplitterNodeParserSemanticSplitterNodeParser按语义相似度断点at semantic breakpoints主题清晰的长文topically varied text
SentenceWindowNodeParserSentenceWindowNodeParser单句为节点+窗口上下文one sentence + window精检索后补上下文precise hit, fuller context

chunk_size / chunk_overlap 的权衡The chunk_size / chunk_overlap trade-off

chunk_size 太大，块里混入大量无关内容，检索噪声多、还挤占 LLM 上下文；而且块再大也不能超过 embedding 模型的 token 上限——常见模型大多在 512 token 左右（详见第 8 课），超出的部分会被悄悄截断、白白丢失。太小，完整语义被切碎，块与块之间断裂、读不成句。chunk_overlap 用少量冗余换“不把一句话切两半”。这对“精准命中 vs 保留上下文”的张力，sentence-window 给了一个漂亮的折中：用单句去检索（足够精准），却把前后句组成的窗口喂给 LLM（补回上下文）。
Too large a chunk_size mixes in lots of irrelevant text — noisy retrieval that also hogs LLM context; and a chunk can never exceed the embedding model's token limit either — most models cap around 512 tokens (see Lesson 8), and anything past that is silently truncated and lost. Too small and a complete thought is shredded, with chunks that break mid-sentence. chunk_overlap trades a little redundancy for “never cut a sentence in half”. For the tension between “precise hits vs. retained context”, sentence-window offers an elegant compromise: retrieve on a single sentence (precise enough), yet feed the LLM the window of surrounding sentences (context restored).
原文按句切分Split text into sentences每个 Node = 一句each Node = one sentence
↓
节点正文 = 单句Node text = a single sentence检索只匹配这一句 → 命中精准retrieval matches just this sentence → precise
↓
metadata['window'] = 前后各 N 句metadata['window'] = ±N sentences查询时替换为窗口 → 补回上下文swapped in at query time → context restored
句窗把“精准检索”和“完整上下文”解耦：检索靠单句，喂给 LLM 靠窗口Sentence-window decouples precise retrieval from full context: retrieve by sentence, feed the window to the LLM
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
node_parser/text/sentence.py · SentenceSplitter — 默认切块器the default splitter
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
node_parser/text/sentence_window.py · SentenceWindowNodeParser.from_defaults — 句窗切块sentence-window parsing
深入：切块策略与旋钮Deep dive: chunking strategies and knobs点击展开expand
🧪 示例：SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512, chunk_overlap=50)🧪 Example: SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512, chunk_overlap=50)
默认切块器按句子把文本凑到约 512 token 一块、相邻块重叠 50 token。这组数值是通用起点：块够大能容下完整语义，重叠又能护住边界句，适合大多数问答场景。
The default splitter packs text into ~512-token chunks along sentence boundaries, with 50 tokens of overlap between neighbours. These values are a solid starting point: chunks large enough to hold a complete thought, with overlap guarding the boundary sentences — good for most Q&A.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
切块本质是在“召回精度”和“上下文完整”之间找平衡：小块检索更准但易断章，大块语义更全但召回更糊。把 chunk_size / chunk_overlap 暴露成旋钮，就是把这个平衡权交给你按数据来调。
Chunking is fundamentally a balance between recall precision and contextual completeness: small chunks retrieve more sharply but fragment meaning; large chunks keep meaning whole but blur recall. Exposing chunk_size / chunk_overlap as knobs hands that balance to you, to tune against your data.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
所有切块器都实现同一个 get_nodes_from_documents 接口。SentenceSplitter 先把文本拆成句子，再贪心地把句子凑到接近 chunk_size，遇到下一块时回退 chunk_overlap 个 token 作为重叠起点。
Every splitter implements the same get_nodes_from_documents interface. SentenceSplitter first breaks text into sentences, then greedily packs sentences up to near chunk_size, backing off by chunk_overlap tokens as the overlapping start of the next chunk.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
TokenTextSplitter 按 token 数硬切，控长最严但可能切断句子；SemanticSplitterNodeParser 在语义断点处下刀，适合主题多变的长文；SentenceWindowNodeParser 用单句检索 + 窗口补上下文，兼顾精准与完整。
TokenTextSplitter cuts strictly by token count — tightest length control but may split sentences; SemanticSplitterNodeParser cuts at semantic breakpoints, good for topically varied text; SentenceWindowNodeParser retrieves by single sentence then restores context via a window — precise and complete at once.
chunk_size / overlap 是 RAG 调优第一旋钮chunk_size / overlap: RAG's first tuning knob
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceSplitter, SentenceWindowNodeParser

splitter = SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512, chunk_overlap=50)
nodes = splitter.get_nodes_from_documents(docs)
print(len(nodes), nodes[0].text[:60])

# 句窗：节点是单句，metadata['window'] 保留前后句作为上下文
window = SentenceWindowNodeParser.from_defaults(window_size=3)
wnodes = window.get_nodes_from_documents(docs)
句窗的完整用法：检索靠单句，喂给 LLM 时再换回窗口Full sentence-window flow: retrieve by sentence, swap the window back before the LLM sees it
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceWindowNodeParser
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import MetadataReplacementPostProcessor

parser = SentenceWindowNodeParser.from_defaults(
    window_size=3, window_metadata_key='window',
    original_text_metadata_key='original_text')
index = VectorStoreIndex(parser.get_nodes_from_documents(docs))

# 检索靠单句命中，喂给 LLM 前再用 window 把上下文换回来
engine = index.as_query_engine(
    similarity_top_k=2,
    node_postprocessors=[MetadataReplacementPostProcessor(target_metadata_key='window')])
print(engine.query('退款多久到账？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 切块决定“检索能命中多准”——RAG 质量的第一旋钮。Chunking decides how precisely retrieval can hit — RAG quality's first knob.
  • chunk_overlap 防止把完整语义从中间切断。chunk_overlap keeps a complete thought from being cut in half.
  • 句窗切块：用单句精准检索，再用窗口补回上下文。Sentence-window: retrieve precisely on a single sentence, then restore context via the window.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
切块器都实现同一个 get_nodes_from_documents 接口，所以换切块策略零成本——这正是“先标准化接口，再谈策略”的威力。
Every splitter implements the same get_nodes_from_documents interface, so swapping strategies is free — the payoff of “standardize the interface first, then vary the strategy”.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. chunk_overlap 的主要作用是？What is the main purpose of chunk_overlap?
  1. 对块去重Deduplicate chunks
  2. 让每个块更大Make each chunk bigger
  3. 相邻块重叠几句，避免语义在边界被切断Overlap adjacent chunks by a few sentences so meaning isn't cut at the boundary
  4. 加快向量化Speed up embedding
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 重叠让跨越块边界的句子/语义不丢失，提升检索召回。Overlap keeps sentences/meaning that straddle a boundary from being lost, improving recall.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你接手一个“答不全 / 跑偏”的 RAG，怀疑是切块。请你来定 chunk_size 与 chunk_overlap：① 依据什么信号、为什么；② 考虑过哪些替代切法、各自取舍；③ 定完用什么指标证明更好？You inherit a RAG that 'under-answers / drifts' and suspect chunking. Set chunk_size and chunk_overlap: (1) by what signal and why; (2) which alternative splitters did you weigh; (3) what metric proves the new split is better?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：按内容结构定大小、受 embedding token 上限约束，并用“改前改后命中率/Faithfulness”证明。① 手册偏小、叙事偏大；太大→噪声多还挤占上下文，太小→语义被切碎；多数 embedding 上限 ~512 token。② 替代：SentenceSplitter(通用)、TokenTextSplitter(严格控长)、SemanticSplitter(按语义断点、贵)、SentenceWindow(检索/上下文解耦)。③ 固定一组带 gold 块的查询，比较改前/改后的检索命中率与Faithfulness，看趋势而非单点。🔑 Key: size by content structure, bounded by the embedding token limit, and prove it with before/after hit-rate / Faithfulness. (1) manuals smaller, narrative larger; too large → noise + context bloat, too small → shredded meaning; most embeddings cap ~512 tokens. (2) Alternatives: SentenceSplitter (general), TokenTextSplitter (strict length), SemanticSplitter (semantic breakpoints, costly), SentenceWindow (decouples retrieval from context). (3) On a fixed gold-chunk query set, compare hit-rate and Faithfulness before vs after — trends, not a single point.
无重叠 overlap=0No overlap
句子被边界切断：块A“…7 个工作” | 块B“日内到账…”，两边都答不全。A sentence cut at the boundary: chunk A '…7 business' | chunk B 'days…' — neither answers fully.
vs
有重叠 overlap=50With overlap
相邻块共享边界句，“7 个工作日内到账”完整落在某块，命中即拿到完整语义。Adjacent chunks share boundary sentences, so the full thought lands in one chunk.
overlap 用少量冗余换“不把一句话切两半”Overlap trades a little redundancy for 'don't cut a thought in half'
🎯 2. sentence-window 怎么同时做到“检索精准”和“上下文完整”？什么场景值得用、代价是什么？How does sentence-window get both precise retrieval and full context at once — and when is it worth the cost?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：它把“检索单位”和“喂给 LLM 的单位”解耦。以单句为 Node 检索(足够精准)，命中后用 MetadataReplacementPostProcessor 把单句换成前后句组成的 window 再交 LLM(补回上下文)。适合“答案靠一句话命中、但要上下文才说得清”的场景；代价是 metadata 变大、要配合特定后处理。🔑 Key: it decouples the retrieval unit from the unit fed to the LLM. Retrieve on single sentences (precise), then on a hit swap the sentence for its surrounding window via MetadataReplacementPostProcessor (restores context). Great when the answer is pinpointed by one sentence but needs context to explain; the cost is larger metadata and a required postprocessor.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 你的文档是 API 手册 vs 小说，chunk_size 该偏大还是偏小？为什么？For an API manual vs a novel, should chunk_size lean larger or smaller? Why?
第二部分 · 写入路径

07 · 元数据与抽取器

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

给 Node 补元数据（标题、关键词、它能回答的问题、摘要）能显著提升检索与过滤。Extractor 用 LLM 自动为每个 Node 生成这些元数据。Enriching Nodes with metadata (title, keywords, the questions it answers, a summary) boosts retrieval and filtering. Extractors use an LLM to generate that metadata per Node automatically.

抽取前 Node.metadataBefore — Node.metadata
检索只能靠正文向量。此刻元数据很稀：{'page': 3}——只有加载时带进来的页码。
Retrieval can only ride on the body vector. Right now the metadata is sparse: {'page': 3} — just the page number carried in at load time.
vs
抽取后 Node.metadataAfter — Node.metadata
抽取器补上三个键：document_title='退款政策'、excerpt_keywords='退款,时效,原路'、questions_this_excerpt_can_answer='退款多久到账？'。这些就是向量之外的第二检索通道：可按字段过滤，也让问句更易对齐。
Extractors add three keys: document_title='Refund policy', excerpt_keywords='refund,timing,original', questions_this_excerpt_can_answer='How long do refunds take?'. That's the second retrieval channel beyond the vector: filterable by field, and far easier to align with a user's question.
抽取前后对照同一个 Node.metadata：抽取器把它从一个页码，填成可过滤、可对齐问句的第二检索通道The same Node.metadata, before and after: extractors grow it from a lone page number into a filterable, question-aligned second retrieval channel
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
给每张便利贴贴上标签和一句摘要：日后既能按主题筛，也能让“问题↔片段”更容易对上。
Put a label and one-line summary on every sticky note: later you can filter by topic and match “question ↔ snippet” far more easily.

常用抽取器Common extractors

抽取器Extractor产出的元数据Metadata it adds
TitleExtractorTitleExtractor文档标题（document_title）a document-level title (document_title)
KeywordExtractorKeywordExtractor关键词keywords
QuestionsAnsweredExtractorQuestionsAnsweredExtractor该片段能回答的问题questions this chunk answers
SummaryExtractorSummaryExtractor片段摘要a chunk summary

元数据 = 检索的第二通道Metadata: retrieval's second channel

向量相似度是第一检索通道，元数据是第二条。一方面，标题、来源、日期这类字段可做精确过滤（“只在某产品手册里检索”）；另一方面，像 questions_this_excerpt_can_answer 这样的字段，把“用户会怎么问”预先写进块里，让“问句”和“片段”在语义空间里更容易对齐、召回更稳。代价是每个 extractor 都要调用一次 LLM，按需启用即可。
Vector similarity is the first retrieval channel; metadata is the second. On one hand, fields like title, source and date enable exact filtering (“search only this product manual”); on the other, fields like questions_this_excerpt_can_answer bake “how users would ask” into the chunk itself, aligning “question ↔ chunk” in semantic space for steadier recall. The cost: each extractor is one LLM call, so enable them selectively.
SentenceSplitterSentenceSplitter
切块 → Nodesplit → Nodes
→
TitleExtractorTitleExtractor
写入 document_titlewrites document_title
→
QuestionsAnsweredExtractorQuestionsAnsweredExtractor
写入 questions_…writes questions_…
transformations 是一条流水线：切块器与抽取器依次加工同一批 Nodetransformations form one assembly line: splitter then extractors process the same Nodes in turn
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
extractors/metadata_extractors.py · TitleExtractor · QuestionsAnsweredExtractor · KeywordExtractor · SummaryExtractor — 都作为 transformation 接入管道all plug in as pipeline transformations
深入：元数据抽取Deep dive: metadata extraction点击展开expand
🧪 示例：用 IngestionPipeline 串起抽取器🧪 Example: chain extractors in an IngestionPipeline
把 SentenceSplitter 与 TitleExtractor、QuestionsAnsweredExtractor 放进 IngestionPipeline(transformations=[...])，run 一次就得到带标题与问题元数据的 Node。
Put SentenceSplitter together with TitleExtractor and QuestionsAnsweredExtractor into IngestionPipeline(transformations=[...]); one run yields Nodes carrying title and question metadata.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
纯向量检索只会“按相似度”召回，遇到同义改写或宽泛提问容易漏。补上元数据这条第二通道，既能按字段过滤缩小范围，又能用“该块能回答的问题”把用户问句和片段对齐，召回更稳、更可控。
Pure vector search only recalls “by similarity” and can miss paraphrases or broad questions. Adding metadata as a second channel lets you both filter by field to narrow scope and align user questions with chunks via “questions this chunk answers” — steadier, more controllable recall.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
每个 extractor 都是一个 transformation，按提示词生成内容并写进固定的 metadata 键（document_title / excerpt_keywords / questions_this_excerpt_can_answer / section_summary）。但调用次数要分两类看：逐块的抽取器（KeywordExtractor / QuestionsAnsweredExtractor / SummaryExtractor）对每个 Node 各调一次 LLM，开销随块数 N 线性增长；文档级的抽取器（如 TitleExtractor）只为每篇文档推断一次标题、再共享给该文档的所有 Node，大致每篇文档一次而非每块一次。所以总开销并不是简单的 N×M——只有逐块抽取器才真正乘以 N。
Each extractor is a transformation that generates content from a prompt and writes it to a fixed metadata key (document_title / excerpt_keywords / questions_this_excerpt_can_answer / section_summary). But the call count splits in two: per-node extractors (KeywordExtractor / QuestionsAnsweredExtractor / SummaryExtractor) make one LLM call per Node, so cost grows linearly with the chunk count N; document-level extractors (e.g. TitleExtractor) infer one title per document and share it across that document's Nodes — roughly once per document, not once per chunk. So the total is not simply N×M — only the per-node extractors truly multiply by N.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
确定性的字段（来源、路径、日期、作者）直接在 Reader 阶段手工写入 metadata，零成本也零误差；只有需要“理解内容”才能得到的字段（标题、关键词、能回答的问题）才值得花 LLM 去抽取。两者常常混用。
Deterministic fields (source, path, date, author) are best written by hand at the Reader stage — free and exact; only fields that require “understanding the content” (title, keywords, answerable questions) are worth an LLM extraction. In practice you mix both.
抽取器即“管道里的一道工序”extractors are just steps in the pipeline
from llama_index.core.extractors import TitleExtractor, QuestionsAnsweredExtractor
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceSplitter
from llama_index.core.ingestion import IngestionPipeline

pipeline = IngestionPipeline(transformations=[
    SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512),
    TitleExtractor(nodes=5),               # 用 LLM 推断标题
    QuestionsAnsweredExtractor(questions=3) # 该块能回答的 3 个问题
])
nodes = pipeline.run(documents=docs)
print(nodes[0].metadata)   # 多了 document_title / questions_this_excerpt_can_answer
手工元数据 + excluded_embed_metadata_keys：让 ID 之类字段不污染向量Hand-written metadata + excluded_embed_metadata_keys: keep fields like IDs out of the vector
from llama_index.core import Document
from llama_index.core.schema import MetadataMode

# 手工写入业务元数据（零 LLM 成本）
doc = Document(
    text='退款将在 7 个工作日内原路退回。',
    metadata={'source': 'faq.md', 'product': 'wallet', 'internal_id': 'X-92'})

# 控制元数据可见性：哪些不进 embedding、哪些不进给 LLM 的 prompt
doc.excluded_embed_metadata_keys = ['internal_id']
doc.excluded_llm_metadata_keys = ['internal_id']
print(doc.get_content(metadata_mode=MetadataMode.EMBED))  # internal_id 不污染向量
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 元数据是检索的第二通道：不止向量相似，还能按标签/来源过滤。Metadata is retrieval's second channel: beyond vector similarity, filter by tag/source.
  • QuestionsAnsweredExtractor 让“问题↔片段”更易对齐。QuestionsAnsweredExtractor aligns “question ↔ chunk” better.
  • 抽取器是 LLM 调用，有成本——按需启用。Extractors call the LLM, so they cost tokens — enable selectively.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
Extractor 与 Splitter 都是 transformation，可任意串联——元数据增强变成管道里可插拔的一环。
Extractors and splitters are both transformations you can chain freely — metadata enrichment becomes a pluggable link in the pipeline.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你想让“用户的问句”更容易命中“陈述句的块”。你会怎么用元数据抽取做到？LLM 抽取成本怎么控？怎么验证召回真的提升？You want users' questions to better hit statement-style chunks. How would metadata extraction help, how do you control LLM cost, and how do you verify recall actually improves?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 QuestionsAnsweredExtractor 预生成“这个块能回答的问题”并一并 embedding，把“问”与“答”在语义空间对齐。成本控制：只对值得的块抽、文档级字段用文档级抽取器(不按块乘)、把确定字段留给 Reader 手写。验证：用真实问句集比较加抽取前后的命中率，确认提升大于成本。🔑 Key: use QuestionsAnsweredExtractor to pre-generate 'questions this chunk answers' and embed them too, aligning question with answer in semantic space. Control cost by extracting only where it pays, using document-level extractors for document-level fields (not multiplied per chunk), and hand-writing deterministic fields at the Reader. Verify by comparing hit-rate on a real question set before vs after, confirming the lift beats the cost.
🎯 2. 哪些 metadata 值得用 LLM 抽、哪些直接在 Reader 阶段手写就够？excluded_embed_metadata_keys 什么时候必须用、为什么？Which metadata is worth an LLM vs hand-writing at the Reader stage, and when must you use excluded_embed_metadata_keys, and why?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：确定性字段(文件名/页码/日期/部门)手写、零成本；只有需要“理解内容”的(摘要/关键词/可回答问题)才花 LLM。excluded_embed_metadata_keys：当某些字段(长 URL、内部 ID、时间戳)会污染语义向量、拉偏相似度时，把它们排除出 embedding——保留用于过滤/展示，但不进向量。🔑 Key: hand-write deterministic fields (filename/page/date/dept) for free; spend an LLM only on fields that require understanding (summary/keywords/answerable questions). Use excluded_embed_metadata_keys when fields (long URLs, internal IDs, timestamps) would pollute the semantic vector and skew similarity — keep them for filtering/display but out of the embedding.

  • LLM 抽取元数据要花钱花时间。对你的语料，哪些元数据值得用 LLM 抽，哪些直接在 Reader 阶段手写就够？LLM metadata extraction costs time and money. For your corpus, which metadata is worth an LLM, and which is fine to hand-write at the Reader stage?
第二部分 · 写入路径

08 · Embedding 向量化

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

Embedding 把文本变成向量，让“语义相近”变成“向量距离近”。检索时把问题也向量化，再找最近的若干 Node。模型由 Settings.embed_model 统一配置。Embeddings turn text into vectors so “semantically similar” becomes “close in vector space”. At query time the question is embedded too, then the nearest Nodes are found. The model is configured globally via Settings.embed_model.

查询query最近邻 top-knearest top-k文档块doc chunks
查询（黄点）落在“退款/退货”一带，top-2 圈出语义最近的退款政策与退货流程，而非字面相同的块。注意：2D 散点只是直觉示意，真正的度量是两个向量的夹角（余弦相似度），而非图上的平面距离The query (amber) lands among “refund / returns”; top-2 circles the two nearest in meaning — refund policy and returns — not literally matching ones. Note: the 2D scatter is only an intuition; the real metric is the angle between the two vectors (cosine similarity), not flat distance on the plane
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
把每段话放到一张语义地图上的坐标；提问就是在地图上落一个点，找最近的几个点。
Place every passage at a coordinate on a semantic map; asking a question drops a point on it and grabs the nearest few.

检索为什么靠向量Why retrieval rides on vectors

做法Approach匹配方式Match by能否懂“同义不同词”Catches paraphrases?
关键词匹配Keyword match字面相同literal overlap不能no
向量检索Vector search语义相近（余弦相似度）semantic closeness (cosine similarity)能yes

同一个 embedding 模型，才有可比的坐标系One embedding model, one comparable space

既然检索靠“向量够不够近”，那“用什么尺子量近”就至关重要。LlamaIndex 默认用余弦相似度，量的是两个向量的夹角——夹角越小越相关。由此引出一个硬约束：查询和文档必须用同一个 embedding 模型。反例很直接——文档用模型 A 向量化、查询却用模型 B，两者落在互不相通的坐标系里，算出来的相似度只是两堆无关数字的巧合，毫无意义。至于换“更强”的模型：通用榜单更高未必在你的领域里召回更好，领域专用或微调过的小模型常常胜过更大的通用模型；而且一旦更换，整个索引都得重新向量化。
Since retrieval hinges on “are the vectors close enough”, what you measure closeness with matters. By default LlamaIndex uses cosine similarity, measuring the angle between two vectors — the smaller the angle, the more related. That implies a hard constraint: the query and the documents must use the same embedding model. The counter-example is stark — embed the documents with model A but the query with model B, and the two live in incompatible coordinate systems; any similarity you compute is a coincidence of unrelated numbers, meaningless. As for switching to a “stronger” model: a higher general-leaderboard score doesn't guarantee better recall in your domain — a domain-specific or fine-tuned smaller model often beats a bigger general one — and any switch forces a full re-embedding of the index.
文本text
一段话或一个问题a passage or a question
→
embed_modelembed_model
查询与文档共用同一个same one for query and docs
→
向量 [1536]vector [1536]
语义的坐标，按余弦比近邻semantic coordinates, compared by cosine
embedding 把文本映射成定长向量；只有查询与文档共用同一个模型，向量才落在同一个坐标系里、夹角才可比Embedding maps text to a fixed-length vector; only when query and documents share one model do the vectors live in the same space and their angle becomes comparable
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
base/embeddings/base.py · BaseEmbedding · similarity · SimilarityMode — 统一接口 + 相似度计算the unified interface + similarity
深入：embedding 与相似度Deep dive: embeddings and similarity点击展开expand
🧪 示例：把一句话变成向量🧪 Example: turn a sentence into a vector
Settings.embed_model.get_text_embedding('退款政策是什么？') 返回一个定长浮点数组（如 1536 维）。同一模型对“退款要多久”给出的向量，会和它在空间里靠得很近。
Settings.embed_model.get_text_embedding('What is the refund policy?') returns a fixed-length float array (e.g. 1536 dims). The same model's vector for “how long do refunds take” lands right next to it in space.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
关键词匹配只认字面，换个说法就失灵。把文本投射到语义向量空间，让“意思相近”而非“用词相同”决定距离，才是语义检索的地基——这也是 RAG 能听懂同义改写的根本原因。
Keyword matching only sees the literal words and breaks on paraphrase. Projecting text into a semantic vector space lets “similar meaning”, not “same wording”, set the distance — the bedrock of semantic search and the reason RAG understands rephrasings at all.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
所有 embedding 实现都遵循 BaseEmbedding 接口：get_text_embedding 给文档用、get_query_embedding 给查询用；检索时用 similarity（默认余弦）给候选打分排序，取分数最高的 top-k。
Every embedding implementation follows the BaseEmbedding interface: get_text_embedding for documents, get_query_embedding for queries; at retrieval time similarity (cosine by default) scores and ranks candidates, keeping the top-k.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
关键词检索（如 BM25）按词频精确命中，擅长专有名词与代码符号，但不懂同义。向量检索懂语义却可能漏掉确切关键词。生产里常把两者混合检索（hybrid）再融合排序，兼得字面精确与语义召回。
Keyword search (e.g. BM25) matches exactly by term frequency — great for proper nouns and code symbols but blind to synonyms. Vector search grasps meaning but may miss an exact keyword. In production you often combine them in hybrid retrieval and fuse the rankings — exact and semantic at once.
一次向量化，多次检索复用embed once, reuse across many queries
from llama_index.core import Settings
from llama_index.embeddings.openai import OpenAIEmbedding

Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(model='text-embedding-3-small')
v = Settings.embed_model.get_text_embedding('退款政策是什么？')
print(len(v))   # 向量维度，如 1536

# 语义越近，余弦相似度越高（检索就按它排序取 top-k）
同义不同词也能算出高相似度——这正是向量检索强于关键词的地方Paraphrases score high even with different words — exactly why vectors beat keywords
from llama_index.core import Settings
from llama_index.embeddings.openai import OpenAIEmbedding

emb = Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(model='text-embedding-3-small')
a = emb.get_text_embedding('退款多久到账？')
b = emb.get_text_embedding('退款需要几天？')      # 近义、不同词
c = emb.get_text_embedding('如何注册新账号？')    # 另一主题

print(round(emb.similarity(a, b), 3))   # 高：语义相近
print(round(emb.similarity(a, c), 3))   # 低：语义无关
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Embedding 把语义相似变成向量距离，是语义检索的地基。Embeddings turn semantic similarity into vector distance — the bedrock of semantic search.
  • 查询与文档必须用同一个 embedding 模型。Query and documents must use the same embedding model.
  • 统一 BaseEmbedding 接口让你随时换模型而不改主链路。The unified BaseEmbedding interface lets you swap models without touching the pipeline.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
embedding 模型是管道里最“牵一发而动全身”的一环：它定义了整套语义坐标系，所以换 LLM、换切块器都只是局部调整，唯独换 embedding 模型必须把全部向量重算一遍——选型要趁早，更要贴合你的领域。
The embedding model is the pipeline's most load-bearing link: it defines the entire semantic coordinate system, so swapping the LLM or the splitter is a local change — but swapping the embedding model forces you to re-embed every vector. Choose it early, and choose it for your domain.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 为什么向量检索能匹配“同义不同词”的内容？Why can vector search match content that's synonymous but uses different words?
  1. 因为用了更大的模型Because it uses a bigger model
  2. 因为大小写不敏感Because it's case-insensitive
  3. 因为 embedding 把语义相近映射成向量距离近Because embeddings map semantic closeness to vector closeness
  4. 因为做了关键词扩展Because it does keyword expansion
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 语义相近的文本向量距离也近，所以即使用词不同也能被召回。Semantically similar text has nearby vectors, so it's recalled even with different wording.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要给法律合同库选 embedding 模型。你会怎么选、为什么不直接用“最大最强”的那个？选定后怎么验证它在这个领域真的好用？Pick an embedding model for a legal-contract corpus. How do you choose, why not just the 'biggest/strongest', and how do you verify it's actually good in this domain?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：领域贴合度 > 通用强度——用你自己的评测集选，而不是默认“更大=更好”。通用最强模型未必懂法律术语；领域/微调模型常反超，还要权衡维度、成本、延迟、是否可私有部署(合同涉密)。验证：建一组带 gold 块的法律问句，比较候选模型的检索命中率/MRR，再看端到端 Faithfulness——用数字选型。🔑 Key: domain fit > raw strength — choose with your own eval set, not 'bigger = better'. The strongest general model may not grasp legal terms; domain/fine-tuned models often win, and you must weigh dimensions, cost, latency, and on-prem deploy (contracts are sensitive). Verify with a legal gold-chunk query set, comparing candidates on hit-rate/MRR and end-to-end Faithfulness — pick by numbers.

🎯 2. 用户搜精确条款编号“X-2000”搜不到——字面明明就在文档里。为什么向量会漏？怎么补救？Users search the exact clause id 'X-2000' and miss it — though it's literally in the docs. Why does the vector miss, and how do you fix it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：向量偏“语义”，对精确符号/罕见 token/编号不敏感，语义上“X-2000”与别的编号很近、可能排不进 top-k。补救：混合检索(向量 + BM25/关键词把精确匹配召回回来)、把编号存进 metadata 做精确过滤、或对这类查询加 rerank。🔑 Key: embeddings capture meaning and are weak on exact symbols/rare tokens/ids — semantically 'X-2000' sits near other ids and may miss top-k. Fixes: hybrid retrieval (vector + BM25/keyword to recover exact matches), store the id in metadata for exact filtering, or add a reranker for such queries.
🎯 3. 你想把 embedding 模型从 A 升级到 B。怎么评估“值不值得升”、怎么安全上线？You want to upgrade the embedding model from A to B. How do you assess whether it's worth it, and how do you roll it out safely?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：升级 embedding ＝ 全量重算向量、坐标系不可比，必须重建索引后再切——不能热替换。评估：在 staging 用 B 重建一份索引，对同一回归集比较命中率/Faithfulness 与延迟成本；只有提升明显才升。上线：双索引灰度，确认 B 不退化再切流量；切换期间查询必须用与建索引相同的模型。🔑 Key: upgrading the embedding means recomputing all vectors into an incomparable space — you must re-index, then cut over; never hot-swap. Assess by rebuilding an index with B in staging and comparing hit-rate/Faithfulness and latency/cost on the same regression set; upgrade only on a clear win. Roll out with dual indexes and a gradual cutover; during the switch, queries must use the same model the index was built with.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 如果上线后想换一个更好的 embedding 模型，需要付出什么代价？这对“多久重建一次索引”有什么启示？If you wanted a better embedding model after launch, what's the cost — and what does that imply about how often you rebuild the index?
第二部分 · 写入路径

09 · 向量存储 Vector Stores

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

向量存哪儿？VectorStore 负责存 Node 的向量+元数据，并支持最近邻查询。默认是内存版 SimpleVectorStore，生产可换 Chroma / FAISS / PG 等，接口一致。Where do the vectors live? A VectorStore stores Node vectors + metadata and supports nearest-neighbor queries. The default is in-memory SimpleVectorStore; in production swap in Chroma / FAISS / PG — same interface.

查询向量Query vector
问题经 embedding 得到the question, embedded
→
VectorStoreVectorStore
近邻搜索 + 元数据过滤nearest-neighbor + metadata filter
→
top-k Nodetop-k Nodes
最相关的若干片段the most relevant chunks
向量库的核心动作：拿查询向量，毫秒级返回最近邻的 top-k 个 NodeA vector store's core move: take a query vector, return the top-k nearest Nodes in milliseconds
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
向量库是语义地图的GPS 索引：给一个坐标，瞬间找出附近的点，而不必逐个比对全图。
A vector store is the GPS index of the semantic map: given a coordinate it finds nearby points instantly, instead of scanning the whole map.

默认 vs 生产Default vs production

场景Scenario选择Choice
学习 / 小数据 / 原型learning / small / prototypeSimpleVectorStore（内存，零依赖）SimpleVectorStore (in-memory)
规模化 / 持久化 / 过滤scale / persistence / filtersChroma · FAISS · pgvector · Qdrant…Chroma · FAISS · pgvector · Qdrant…

VectorStore 的职责与可替换性What a VectorStore owns, and why it's swappable

VectorStore 干三件事：保存每个 Node 的向量、保存其元数据、并支持“给定一个查询向量、返回最近邻”。LlamaIndex 把这三件事抽象成统一契约，于是笔记本上的内存库和生产级引擎对上层看起来一模一样。你按 SimpleVectorStore 写通的代码，换成 Chroma 只动注入 StorageContext 的那几行，检索逻辑、索引、查询引擎全都不变。
A VectorStore does three things: store each Node's vector, store its metadata, and answer “given a query vector, return the nearest neighbours”. LlamaIndex abstracts these into one contract, so a laptop's in-memory store and a production engine look identical upstream. Code you got working on SimpleVectorStore moves to Chroma by changing only the few lines that inject the StorageContext — retrieval, index and query engine all stay the same.
内存 SimpleVectorStoreIn-memory SimpleVectorStore
零依赖，随进程而生灭；线性扫描全部向量，返回的是精确最近邻。适合学习、原型与小数据。
Zero-dependency, lives and dies with the process; a linear scan over every vector returns the exact nearest neighbours. Great for learning, prototypes and small data.
vs
生产向量库 Chroma · FAISS · pgvectorProduction store: Chroma · FAISS · pgvector
持久化、可扩展，用 ANN（近似最近邻）索引和元数据过滤，百万级向量也能毫秒级返回。代价是“近似”：用一点召回率换巨大的速度，命中率可调但并非 100%。
Persistent and scalable; an ANN (approximate nearest-neighbor) index plus metadata filters answer in milliseconds even at millions of vectors. The catch is “approximate”: it trades a little recall for huge speed, so hit rate is tunable, not a guaranteed 100%.
同一个 VectorStore 接口，两种实现：上线只是换实现，不是重写One VectorStore interface, two impls: going live is a swap, not a rewrite
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
vector_stores/simple.py · SimpleVectorStore — 默认内存向量库the default in-memory store
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
vector_stores/types.py · VectorStoreQuery — 统一的相似度查询契约the unified similarity-query contract
深入：向量库的统一契约Deep dive: the vector store's unified contract点击展开expand
🧪 示例：默认内存库 vs 注入 Chroma🧪 Example: in-memory default vs injecting Chroma
VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs) 默认用内存 SimpleVectorStore；要换 Chroma，只需构造 ChromaVectorStore、用 StorageContext.from_defaults(vector_store=...) 注入，其余代码原样不动。
VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs) uses the in-memory SimpleVectorStore by default; to switch to Chroma you only build a ChromaVectorStore and inject it via StorageContext.from_defaults(vector_store=...) — everything else stays put.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把“近邻搜索”收敛成一个统一接口，意味着你能在不重写检索逻辑的前提下，从笔记本无缝升级到生产引擎——选向量库变成一个纯运维/规模问题，而非代码架构问题。
Collapsing nearest-neighbor search into one interface lets you upgrade from laptop to production engine without rewriting retrieval logic — picking a store becomes an ops/scale decision, not an architectural one.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
上层把查询打包成 VectorStoreQuery（含 query_embedding、similarity_top_k 与可选 filters），交给具体向量库执行，返回命中的 Node 与分数。各家库实现各异，但都满足这同一份契约。
The layer above packs a query into a VectorStoreQuery (carrying query_embedding, similarity_top_k and optional filters) and hands it to the concrete store, which returns matching Nodes with scores. Each store implements it differently but all honour the same contract.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
Chroma 上手简单、本地友好；FAISS 极快但偏库而非服务；pgvector 复用现成 Postgres、便于事务与运维；Qdrant / Weaviate 等是云原生向量服务。取舍点在规模、过滤能力、运维成本与是否需要持久化。
Chroma is easy and local-friendly; FAISS is blazingly fast but a library, not a service; pgvector reuses your existing Postgres for transactions and ops; Qdrant / Weaviate are cloud-native vector services. You trade off scale, filtering, ops cost and whether you need persistence.
从内存到生产库，主链路不变in-memory → production, pipeline unchanged
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, StorageContext

# 默认：内存 SimpleVectorStore
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)

# 换生产向量库（接口一致，只改这几行）
# pip install llama-index-vector-stores-chroma chromadb
import chromadb
from llama_index.vector_stores.chroma import ChromaVectorStore
store = ChromaVectorStore(chroma_collection=chromadb.Client().create_collection('rag'))
sc = StorageContext.from_defaults(vector_store=store)
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs, storage_context=sc)
把近邻搜索和元数据过滤组合，检索更准也更可控Combine nearest-neighbor with metadata filters for tighter, more controllable retrieval
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex
from llama_index.core.vector_stores import (
    MetadataFilters, MetadataFilter, FilterOperator)

index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)

# 近邻搜索 + 元数据过滤：只在 source='faq' 且 year >= 2024 的块里找
flt = MetadataFilters(filters=[
    MetadataFilter(key='source', value='faq'),
    MetadataFilter(key='year', value=2024, operator=FilterOperator.GTE),
])
engine = index.as_query_engine(similarity_top_k=3, filters=flt)
print(engine.query('最新的退款政策？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • VectorStore = 存向量 + 元数据 + 近邻查询。A VectorStore = stores vectors + metadata + nearest-neighbor search.
  • 默认内存库适合学习；生产换集成库，接口一致。The in-memory default suits learning; production swaps integrations with the same interface.
  • 通过 StorageContext 注入向量库。Inject the store via StorageContext.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把“近邻搜索”抽象成 VectorStoreQuery，让笔记本内存版和生产级向量库对上层完全一样——上线只是换实现，不是重写。
Abstracting nearest-neighbor search as VectorStoreQuery makes the laptop store and a production engine look identical upstream — going live is a swap, not a rewrite.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 从内存版 SimpleVectorStore 换成 Chroma，主要需要改什么？To switch from the in-memory SimpleVectorStore to Chroma, what mainly changes?
