  3. 只需通过 StorageContext 注入新的向量库Just inject the new store via StorageContext
  4. 必须更换 embedding 模型You must change the embedding model
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C VectorStore 接口统一，换实现只改注入这一步，主链路不动。The VectorStore interface is uniform; swapping implementations only changes the injection — the pipeline stays.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要从内存版 SimpleVectorStore 迁到生产向量库。按什么标准选？“百万级毫秒查询”靠什么、代价是什么？怎么验证召回没因近似而垮？You're moving from the in-memory SimpleVectorStore to a production store. By what criteria? How do you get 'millisecond queries at million-scale', at what cost, and how do you verify recall didn't collapse from the approximation?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：靠 ANN(近似最近邻)换速度，召回率可调、并非 100%——要用评测把召回卡在可接受线。选型标准：规模/持久化、metadata 过滤、库 vs 服务、事务一致性、运维成本(FAISS 快但偏库；pgvector 复用 Postgres+事务；Chroma 开箱)。验证：对一组 gold 查询比较 ANN 与精确扫描的命中率差，调 ANN 参数把召回拉回阈值，再看延迟是否仍达标。🔑 Key: speed comes from ANN (approximate NN); recall is tunable, not 100% — pin it above an acceptable line with evals. Criteria: scale/persistence, metadata filtering, library-vs-service, transactions, ops (FAISS fast but library-ish; pgvector reuses Postgres + transactions; Chroma batteries-included). Verify by comparing ANN vs exact-scan hit-rate on gold queries, tuning ANN params back to threshold, then checking latency still holds.
🎯 2. 既要语义检索、又要“只在某部门 / 某年份里找”，你会怎么实现？You need semantic search AND 'only within a dept / year' — how do you implement it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 MetadataFilters 先把范围约束到对的子集，再在子集里做向量近邻——“先按标签筛、再按语义排”。前提是建索引时就把部门/年份写进每个 Node 的 metadata，且所选向量库支持过滤下推(否则要先取再过滤、效率差)。🔑 Key: use MetadataFilters to constrain to the right subset, then do vector NN within it — 'filter by tag, then rank by meaning'. It requires writing dept/year into each Node's metadata at index time, and a store that supports filter push-down (else you fetch-then-filter, which is inefficient).
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 从内存版 SimpleVectorStore 迁到生产向量库，你会用哪些标准来选（规模、过滤、事务、运维）？Moving from the in-memory SimpleVectorStore to a production vector DB, what criteria would you choose by (scale, filtering, transactions, ops)?
第二部分 · 写入路径

10 · 索引 Index 抽象

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

Index 不只是“向量库”——它是为某种检索方式组织 Node 的数据结构。不同 Index 对应不同问题：相似问答用 VectorStoreIndex，整库总结用 SummaryIndex，实体关系用 PropertyGraphIndex。An Index isn't just a vector store — it's a data structure that organizes Nodes for a particular way of retrieving. Different Indexes fit different questions: VectorStoreIndex for similarity Q&A, SummaryIndex for whole-corpus summaries, PropertyGraphIndex for entity relations.

IndexIndex
组织方式Organizes by
适合Best for
VectorStoreIndexVectorStoreIndex
向量空间近邻nearest-neighbor in vector space
相似问答similarity Q&A
SummaryIndexSummaryIndex
线性 Node 列表a linear list of Nodes
整库总结whole-corpus summary
DocumentSummaryIndexDocumentSummaryIndex
每篇文档一份摘要one summary per document
多文档路由routing across docs
PropertyGraphIndexPropertyGraphIndex
实体-关系图an entity-relation graph
多跳/关系推理multi-hop / relations
四种 Index = 四种组织 Node 的方式，各自擅长一类问题Four Indexes = four ways to organize Nodes, each best at one kind of question
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
同一堆资料的不同组织法：词典（按相似度近邻）、章节大纲（逐条遍历总结）、知识图谱（按实体关系跳转）。
Different organizations of the same pile: a dictionary (nearest-neighbor), a chapter outline (walk every entry to summarize), a knowledge graph (hop by entity relations).

同一个问题，两种 Index 两种答案One question, two Indexes, two answers

选错 Index，再好的数据也答非所问。拿同一句问题分别问两种最常见的索引，差别一目了然：
Pick the wrong Index and even great data answers the wrong question. Put the same question to the two most common Indexes and the difference is obvious:
VectorStoreIndexVectorStoreIndex
把问题向量化，只定点召回最相关的 top-k 段再作答：回答“退款多久到账？”这类具体细节又快又准；但问“整份资料讲了什么”时，只看几段容易以偏概全。
Embeds the question and answers from just the top-k most similar chunks: fast and precise for specifics like “how long do refunds take?”, but asked “what does the whole corpus cover?” it sees only a few chunks and tends to generalize from a fragment.
vs
SummaryIndexSummaryIndex
不挑不选，遍历全部 Node 逐步归纳：天生适合“总结全库”“这批文档讲了什么”；代价是每次都读全量，问具体细节时既慢又贵。
Picks nothing — it walks every Node and synthesizes: a natural fit for “summarize the whole corpus” / “what do these docs cover”; the cost is reading everything each time, so it's slow and pricey for narrow questions.
同一句问题，两种 Index 给出不同答案：向量索引定点召回最相关几段，摘要索引遍历全库做归纳Same question, two Indexes, two answers: the vector index pinpoints the most relevant chunks; the summary index walks the whole corpus to synthesize

选 Index = 选检索范式Choosing an Index = choosing a retrieval paradigm

Index 决定的不是“存哪儿”，而是“怎么找”。VectorStoreIndex 把 Node 摆进向量空间、按相似度近邻召回；SummaryIndex 把 Node 排成一列、逐条遍历做全局总结；PropertyGraphIndex 把 Node 连成实体关系图、按边跳转做多跳推理。同一堆资料，选不同 Index 就得到不同的检索范式——而它们都用 from_documents / as_query_engine 的同款入口，让你能用同一套代码切换甚至组合。
An Index decides not “where things live” but “how you find them”. VectorStoreIndex places Nodes in vector space and recalls by similarity; SummaryIndex lines Nodes up and walks them all for a global summary; PropertyGraphIndex links Nodes into an entity-relation graph and hops along edges for multi-hop reasoning. Same pile of data, different Index, different retrieval paradigm — yet all share the from_documents / as_query_engine entry points, so you switch or even combine them with the same code.

→

→
RouterQueryEngineRouterQueryEngine
按问题自动选 Indexauto-pick an Index per question
不同 Index 共用同一个 as_query_engine 入口，还能用 Router 在它们之间分流Every Index shares the same as_query_engine entry; a Router can even dispatch between them
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
indices/vector_store/base.py · VectorStoreIndex — 最常用的相似检索索引the common similarity index
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
indices/list/base.py · SummaryIndex — 遍历式索引（原 ListIndex）the iterate-all index (formerly ListIndex)
深入：Index 抽象Deep dive: the Index abstraction点击展开expand
🧪 示例：VectorStoreIndex vs SummaryIndex🧪 Example: VectorStoreIndex vs SummaryIndex
同一批 docs，VectorStoreIndex 适合“退款政策是什么”这类定点问答（按相似度取 top-k）；SummaryIndex 适合“全文讲了什么”这类整库总结（遍历所有 Node 再归纳）。
On the same docs, VectorStoreIndex suits pinpoint questions like “what's the refund policy” (top-k by similarity), while SummaryIndex suits whole-corpus asks like “what does the text cover” (walk every Node, then summarize).
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
不同问题需要不同的“组织 + 检索”策略：定点问答要近邻、全局总结要遍历、关系推理要图。把它们做成可互换的 Index，就能用同一套上层代码服务截然不同的问法。
Different questions need different “organize + retrieve” strategies: pinpoint Q&A wants nearest-neighbor, global summary wants iteration, relational reasoning wants a graph. Making them interchangeable Indexes lets one upper layer serve very different question shapes.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
所有 Index 都继承 BaseIndex，共享 from_documents（建索引）与 as_query_engine / as_retriever（装配查询）。差异只在于内部如何组织 Node、以及默认配哪种 retriever 与 response 合成策略。
Every Index inherits BaseIndex, sharing from_documents (build) and as_query_engine / as_retriever (assemble queries). They differ only in how they organize Nodes internally and which default retriever and response strategy they wire up.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
当一个库里既有定点问答又有整库总结时，可建多个 Index，再用 RouterQueryEngine 按问题自动路由到合适的那个；也可以组合检索器、做多 Index 融合。单一 Index 简单，多 Index + Router 更全能。
When a corpus needs both pinpoint Q&A and global summaries, build several Indexes and let a RouterQueryEngine auto-route each question to the right one; you can also compose retrievers and fuse multiple Indexes. One Index is simpler; many Indexes + a Router is more capable.
选 Index 就是选检索范式choosing an Index = choosing a retrieval style
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, SummaryIndex

vindex = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs)   # 相似问答
print(vindex.as_query_engine().query('退款政策？'))

sindex = SummaryIndex.from_documents(docs)        # 整库总结
print(sindex.as_query_engine(response_mode='tree_summarize').query('全文讲了什么？'))
多 Index + Router：让框架按问题自动选检索范式Many Indexes + a Router: let the framework auto-pick the retrieval paradigm per question
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, SummaryIndex
from llama_index.core.tools import QueryEngineTool
from llama_index.core.query_engine import RouterQueryEngine

vector_tool = QueryEngineTool.from_defaults(
    VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(docs).as_query_engine(),
    description='按相似度回答具体细节问题')
summary_tool = QueryEngineTool.from_defaults(
    SummaryIndex.from_documents(docs).as_query_engine(response_mode='tree_summarize'),
    description='对全文做整体总结')

# Router 读 description，自动把问题分给合适的 Index
engine = RouterQueryEngine.from_defaults([vector_tool, summary_tool])
print(engine.query('全文主要讲了什么？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Index = 组织方式 + 检索范式，不等于向量库本身。An Index = organization + retrieval style, not the vector store itself.
  • 相似问答选 VectorStoreIndex；整库总结选 SummaryIndex。VectorStoreIndex for similarity Q&A; SummaryIndex for whole-corpus summaries.
  • 所有 Index 都用 from_documents / as_query_engine 同款入口。Every Index shares the from_documents / as_query_engine entry points.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
“选 Index”本质是“选检索策略”。统一的 Index→QueryEngine 入口让你用同一套代码切换范式，甚至用 Router 在多个 Index 间自动路由。
“Choosing an Index” is really “choosing a retrieval strategy.” The uniform Index→QueryEngine entry lets you switch paradigms with the same code — even auto-route across indexes with a Router.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

  1. 关键词匹配Keyword matching
  2. SummaryIndex（遍历所有 Node）SummaryIndex (iterates over all Nodes)
  3. VectorStoreIndex（top-k 近邻）VectorStoreIndex (top-k nearest neighbors)
  4. 换一个更大的模型Switch to a bigger model
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 总结需要覆盖全部内容，SummaryIndex 遍历所有 Node，而 VectorStoreIndex 只取 top-k。Summarizing must cover everything; SummaryIndex iterates all Nodes, whereas VectorStoreIndex only takes top-k.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 一个库里既有定点 FAQ、又要“整库总结”。你会怎么组织 Index？为什么一个 Index 难兼顾两种范式？怎么验证路由把问题送对了？One base needs both pinpoint FAQ and 'summarize the whole base'. How do you organize the Index, why can't one Index do both, and how do you verify routing sends each question to the right one?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：建多个 Index(向量索引 + 摘要索引)，用 RouterQueryEngine 按问题路由。因为“Index = 怎么找”：向量索引按相似度定点召回，摘要索引遍历全部——一个结构难同时擅长两种检索行为。验证：构造“定点类 vs 总结类”问题各一批，检查路由选择的命中率(选错就调 selector/描述)，再看各自端到端答案质量。🔑 Key: build multiple indices (vector + summary) and route by question with a RouterQueryEngine. Because 'Index = how you find': a vector index pinpoints by similarity, a summary index walks everything — one structure can't excel at both. Verify with a batch of pinpoint vs summary questions, checking routing accuracy (tune the selector/descriptions on mistakes), then each path's end-to-end answer quality.

🎯 2. 需求从“单库 FAQ”演进到“跨 5 条产品线、还要多跳推理（A 依赖 B、B 依赖 C）”。你会怎么调整 Index 选型？为什么纯向量检索在多跳上吃力、怎么验证？Requirements grow from 'single-base FAQ' to 'across 5 product lines with multi-hop reasoning (A depends on B depends on C)'. How do you adjust your Index choice, why does pure vector retrieval struggle with multi-hop, and how would you verify?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：多跳/关系推理超出“按相似度取 top-k”的能力——考虑 PropertyGraphIndex（实体-关系图）或多 Index + Router 分流。纯向量把每跳当独立检索，难把 A→B→C 串成链路；跨产品线则用 metadata 过滤或按线建多个 Index。验证：构造需要 2+ 跳才能答对的问题集，比较向量索引 vs 图索引的正确率。🔑 Key: multi-hop/relational reasoning exceeds 'top-k by similarity' — consider a PropertyGraphIndex (entity-relation graph) or multiple indices + a Router. Pure vectors treat each hop as independent retrieval and can't chain A→B→C; across product lines, use metadata filters or per-line indices. Verify with a question set needing 2+ hops, comparing the correctness of the vector index vs the graph index.

第二部分 · 写入路径

11 · Ingestion 管道与持久化

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

IngestionPipeline 把切块、抽取、向量化串成一条可缓存、可去重的管道，重复运行只处理变化的部分。索引建好后，用 storage_context.persist 整体落盘，下次用顶层函数 load_index_from_storage（传入 StorageContext）秒开，免去每次重建。An IngestionPipeline chains splitting, extraction and embedding into a cacheable, dedup-aware pipeline, so re-runs only touch what changed. Once the index is built, storage_context.persist writes it to disk, and the top-level load_index_from_storage (given a StorageContext) reloads it instantly — no rebuild next time.

相同输入命中、不重算same input hits cache, skips recompute

按内容哈希增量更新incremental by content hash
一条摄取管道：transformations 依次加工，cache 跳过重复计算，docstore 按文档去重One ingestion pipeline: transformations process in turn, the cache skips repeats, the docstore dedups by document
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
Ingestion 像自动化装配线（切块→抽取→向量化），缓存让“已加工的零件”不重做；persist 像把建好的图书馆整体存档，下次直接开门营业。
Ingestion is an assembly line (split→extract→embed); the cache skips “parts already made”; persist archives the finished library so next time you just open the doors.

管道 + 存储解决什么What pipeline + storage solve

能力Capability带来的好处Benefit
transformations 串联chained transformations一处定义、可复用define once, reuse
cachecache相同输入不重复算skip recompute on same input
docstore 去重docstore dedup增量更新只处理变化的文档incremental: only changed docs
persist / loadpersist / load索引落盘，重启免重建index on disk, no rebuild on restart

把建索引做成幂等、可缓存的管道Make indexing an idempotent, cacheable pipeline

demo 里“每次重跑都全量重建”尚可忍受，生产里却致命：数据天天变，全量重算既慢又贵。IngestionPipeline 把摄取做成幂等管道——run 时对每个转换的输入算内容哈希，命中缓存就跳过；配上 docstore，相同文档不重复处理，只有变化的文档才走完整流程。再用 persist / load 把成品索引落盘，重启免重建。这三件事合起来，才让 RAG 从“能跑通”走到“可维护”。
“Rebuild everything on every run” is tolerable in a demo but fatal in production: data changes daily and full recomputation is slow and costly. IngestionPipeline makes ingestion idempotent — on run it hashes each transformation's input and skips on a cache hit; paired with a docstore, identical documents aren't reprocessed and only changed docs run the full path. Then persist / load put the finished index on disk so restarts skip the rebuild. Together these three take RAG from “it runs” to “it's maintainable”.
persist(persist_dir)persist(persist_dir)把内存中的索引整体写到磁盘writes the in-memory index to disk
docstore.jsondocstore.jsonNode 正文与元数据Node text and metadata
index_store.jsonindex_store.json索引结构（谁指向谁）the index structure (what points to what)
vector_store.jsonvector_store.json向量数据the vectors
load_index_from_storageload_index_from_storage从三件套重建索引，秒级开门rebuilds the index from the three — open in seconds
persist 把索引拆成磁盘上的三件套，load 再把它们拼回可查询的索引；不过生产里若向量交给外部库（Chroma / pgvector）托管，向量就不在本地，落盘的往往只剩 docstore 与 index_storepersist splits the index into three local files; load stitches them back into a queryable index. In production, though, if the vectors live in an external store (Chroma / pgvector) they aren't local — often only the docstore and index_store hit disk

深入：摄取管道与持久化Deep dive: the ingestion pipeline and persistence点击展开expand
🧪 示例：带 docstore 的 IngestionPipeline🧪 Example: an IngestionPipeline with a docstore
IngestionPipeline(transformations=[...], docstore=SimpleDocumentStore()) 第一次 run 会完整处理所有文档；之后再 run，未变化的文档直接命中缓存/去重，只有新增或改动的文档才重新加工。
IngestionPipeline(transformations=[...], docstore=SimpleDocumentStore()) processes every document on the first run; on later runs unchanged documents hit the cache/dedup, and only new or modified documents are reprocessed.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
生产数据是活的：每天只有一小部分变化。幂等 + 缓存 + 去重让“重建索引”的代价正比于变化量而非总量，既省钱又省时，还保证重复运行结果一致。
Production data is alive: only a small slice changes each day. Idempotency + cache + dedup make the cost of “rebuilding the index” proportional to the delta, not the total — cheaper, faster, and consistent across repeated runs.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
run 时，管道对每个转换的（输入 Node + 转换配置）算一个哈希作为缓存键，命中就复用上次结果；docstore 则按 doc_id 记录每个文档的内容哈希，配合 DocstoreStrategy 决定是 UPSERT 还是跳过。
On run, the pipeline hashes each transformation's (input Nodes + config) into a cache key and reuses last time's output on a hit; the docstore records each document's content hash by doc_id and, via a DocstoreStrategy, decides whether to UPSERT or skip.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
不用管道也能跑：每次都 from_documents 全量重建。小数据时无所谓，但随着库变大，全量重算的时间和 embedding 费用会线性膨胀——这正是增量摄取存在的理由。
You can skip the pipeline and just from_documents from scratch every time. Fine for small data, but as the corpus grows the recompute time and embedding bill scale linearly — exactly why incremental ingestion exists.
建一次、存起来、反复用build once, persist, reuse
from llama_index.core import VectorStoreIndex, StorageContext, load_index_from_storage
from llama_index.core.ingestion import IngestionPipeline
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceSplitter
from llama_index.core.storage.docstore import SimpleDocumentStore

# 可缓存 + 去重的摄取管道：相同输入不重算，相同文档不重复处理
pipeline = IngestionPipeline(
    transformations=[SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512)],
    docstore=SimpleDocumentStore(),   # 配 docstore 才能按文档去重做增量
)
nodes = pipeline.run(documents=docs)
index = VectorStoreIndex(nodes)

# 落盘，下次秒开
index.storage_context.persist(persist_dir='./storage')
index2 = load_index_from_storage(StorageContext.from_defaults(persist_dir='./storage'))
第二次 run 只处理变化的文档，其余命中缓存/去重——这就是增量摄取The second run touches only changed docs; the rest hit cache/dedup — that's incremental ingestion
from llama_index.core import Document
from llama_index.core.ingestion import IngestionPipeline, IngestionCache
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceSplitter
from llama_index.core.storage.docstore import SimpleDocumentStore

pipeline = IngestionPipeline(
    transformations=[SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512)],
    docstore=SimpleDocumentStore(),   # 去重：按 doc_id + 内容哈希判断是否变化
    cache=IngestionCache(),           # 缓存：相同输入直接复用上次结果
)

docs = [Document(text='退款政策……', doc_id='faq-1')]
print(len(pipeline.run(documents=docs)))   # 首次：完整处理

docs = [Document(text='退款政策（已更新）……', doc_id='faq-1')]   # 同一 doc_id、内容已更新
print(len(pipeline.run(documents=docs)))   # 再跑：仅这篇重算，其余命中缓存
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • IngestionPipeline 让“建索引”变成幂等、可缓存的管道。IngestionPipeline makes “building the index” an idempotent, cacheable process.
  • docstore 去重支持增量更新：只处理变化的文档。docstore dedup enables incremental updates: only changed docs are processed.
  • persist / load_index_from_storage 避免每次启动都重建。persist / load_index_from_storage avoid rebuilding on every startup.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把摄取做成幂等可缓存的管道，是 RAG 从“demo 跑通”走向“生产可维护”的关键一步——数据天天变，但只重算变化的部分。
Making ingestion an idempotent, cacheable pipeline is the step that takes RAG from “demo works” to “maintainable in production” — data changes daily, but only the deltas are recomputed.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 文档每天小幅更新，如何避免每次全量重建索引？Documents change a little every day — how do you avoid fully rebuilding the index each time?
  1. 换更快的机器Use a faster machine
  2. 用 IngestionPipeline 的缓存 + docstore 去重做增量Use IngestionPipeline's cache + docstore dedup for incremental updates
  3. 改用关键词检索Switch to keyword search
  4. 关掉切块Turn off chunking
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 缓存让相同输入不重复计算，docstore 去重让只处理新增/变化的文档。The cache skips recomputing identical inputs, and docstore dedup processes only new/changed documents.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 知识库每天只变 1%。你怎么把建索引做成增量、幂等、可缓存的管道？怎么验证“只重算了变化的那部分”？Your base changes 1% a day. How do you make indexing an incremental, idempotent, cacheable pipeline, and how do you verify only the changed part was recomputed?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 IngestionPipeline + docstore + DocstoreStrategy，让代价正比于“变化量”而非总量。未变的块按内容哈希命中缓存、被去重，只有变化的文档触发重新切块/向量化；前提是文档有稳定 ref_doc_id。验证：改一篇文档再 run，看日志/计数确认只处理了那一篇、其余命中缓存(耗时与变更量成正比)。🔑 Key: use IngestionPipeline + a docstore + DocstoreStrategy so cost is proportional to the delta, not the total. Unchanged chunks hit the content-hash cache and are deduped; only changed docs trigger re-split/re-embed — given stable ref_doc_ids. Verify by editing one doc, re-running, and checking logs/counts that only that doc was processed while the rest hit cache (time scales with the change).

🎯 2. persist 到底存了哪三件？换成生产向量库(Chroma/pgvector)后有什么不同、加载时要注意什么？What three things does persist write, and how does that change with a production store (Chroma/pgvector) — what must you watch on load?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：默认三件套——docstore(Node 内容)、index store(索引结构)、vector store(向量)。换生产库后，向量由外部数据库托管，本地不再是 vector_store.json；加载时 StorageContext 必须连回同一个库，且查询用与建索引相同的 embedding 模型。🔑 Key: by default three pieces — docstore (Node content), index store (index structure), vector store (vectors). With a production store the vectors live in an external DB, not a local vector_store.json; on load the StorageContext must reconnect to the same store, and queries must use the same embedding model the index was built with.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 如果知识库每天只变动 1%，“每次全量重建”与“增量摄取”在成本和复杂度上如何取舍？If your knowledge base changes 1% a day, how do you trade off 'full rebuild each time' vs 'incremental ingestion' in cost and complexity?
第三部分 · 查询路径

12 · 检索器 Retrievers

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

查询路径的第一步：Retriever 把问题向量化，去索引里取回最相关的 top-k 个 Node（带相似度分数的 NodeWithScore）。index.as_retriever() 是入口，此刻还没调用 LLM。First stop of the query path: a Retriever embeds the question and fetches the most relevant top-k Nodes (scored NodeWithScore). index.as_retriever() is the entry point — no LLM has been called yet.

好召回Good recall
问「退款政策是什么？」→ retrieve() 取回 top-3：
0.89 退款政策条款 ✓
0.86 退款到账时限 ✓
0.83 退款申请流程 ✓
三块全相关、分数高，正确依据都在 top-k 里。
Ask “What's the refund policy?” → retrieve() returns top-3:
0.89 refund-policy clause ✓
0.86 refund timing ✓
0.83 how to file a refund ✓
all relevant, all high-scoring — the right evidence sits in the top-k.
vs
坏召回Bad recall
同一个问题，却取回：
0.71 配送时效 ✗ 跑题
0.55 账户注册 ✗ 跑题
0.31 退款政策条款 —— 正确块分数偏低、险些没进 top-k
无关块挤进来、正确依据沉到末尾，召回失准。
Same query, yet it fetches:
0.71 delivery times ✗ off-topic
0.55 account signup ✗ off-topic
0.31 refund-policy clause — the right chunk, scoring low, barely in the top-k
noise crowds in and the right evidence sinks to the bottom — recall is off.
不调用 LLM，只看 retrieve() 的结果就能判断召回好坏Without calling the LLM, you can judge recall from retrieve()'s results alone
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
图书管理员按你的主题取回最相关的几页，整齐摆在桌上——但还没开始替你写答案。
The librarian brings back the few most relevant pages and lays them out — but hasn't started writing your answer yet.

检索的关键旋钮The key retrieval knob

概念Concept含义Meaning
similarity_top_ksimilarity_top_k取回多少个最相近 Nodehow many nearest Nodes to fetch
NodeWithScoreNodeWithScoreNode + 相似度分数a Node plus its similarity score
QueryBundleQueryBundle封装查询（文本/向量）wraps the query (text/embedding)
top_k 太小top_k too small
只取回 1–2 个块，容易漏掉真正相关的内容，答案残缺。
Fetching only 1–2 chunks risks missing the truly relevant content, so the answer comes out incomplete.
vs
top_k 太大top_k too large
取回过多块会混入无关噪声，既增加成本，也可能稀释真正的答案。
Fetching too many chunks lets in irrelevant noise, raising cost and potentially diluting the real answer.
similarity_top_k 是召回与噪声之间的平衡旋钮（常从 3–5 起步）similarity_top_k balances recall against noise (often start at 3–5)

为什么把检索单独拎出来Why isolate retrieval as its own step

检索与生成解耦后，“召回对不对”可以脱离 LLM 单独度量：直接看 retrieve() 返回的 Node 是否包含正确依据。于是调相似度阈值、换检索器、改 top_k 都能立刻验证，而不必每次都跑一遍昂贵的生成。
Once retrieval is decoupled from generation, “did we recall the right content?” can be measured without the LLM at all: just inspect whether the Nodes from retrieve() contain the right evidence. Tuning the cutoff, swapping retrievers or changing top_k is then verified instantly, without paying for generation every time.
这正是把检索单列一课的原因：命中率（hit-rate）、MRR 这类指标只对 retrieve() 的输出打分，完全不跑生成。召回这关没过，再强的 LLM 也只是在错误的资料上一本正经地作答；先把“取回对的内容”调好，后面的后处理与合成才谈得上意义。
That's exactly why retrieval earns a lesson of its own: metrics like hit-rate or MRR score only the output of retrieve(), never running generation. If recall fails, even the strongest LLM merely reasons fluently over the wrong material; get “fetch the right content” right first, and only then do post-processing and synthesis even matter.

indices/vector_store/retrievers/retriever.py · VectorIndexRetriever — 向量索引的检索器the vector-index retriever
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
base/base_retriever.py · BaseRetriever.retrieve — 所有检索器的统一入口the unified entry point every retriever shares
深入：检索这一步的里里外外Deep dive: the ins and outs of retrieval点击展开expand
🧪 示例：只检索不生成🧪 Example: retrieve without generating
index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=3).retrieve('…') 返回 List[NodeWithScore]，你可以直接打印分数和文本，确认召回是否命中——完全不碰 LLM。
index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=3).retrieve('…') returns a List[NodeWithScore]; print the scores and text to confirm the recall hit — without touching the LLM.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把检索独立成一等公民，你就能单独评估与优化召回，再分别优化生成，两个问题不再纠缠。
Making retrieval a first-class citizen lets you evaluate and optimize recall on its own, then optimize generation separately — the two problems stop entangling.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
BaseRetriever.retrieve() 是模板方法：它处理 QueryBundle 等通用逻辑，再调用各子类实现的 _retrieve()（如 VectorIndexRetriever 做向量近邻搜索）。
BaseRetriever.retrieve() is a template method: it handles shared logic like the QueryBundle, then calls each subclass's _retrieve() (e.g. VectorIndexRetriever does vector nearest-neighbor search).
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
除了向量检索，还有关键词检索（BM25）、知识图谱检索，以及把多者融合的混合检索——它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever 接口，可直接替换。
Beyond vector search there's keyword retrieval (BM25), knowledge-graph retrieval, and hybrid retrieval that fuses several — all implementing the same BaseRetriever interface, so they drop in interchangeably.
检索独立于生成，可单独评估retrieval is separate from generation — evaluate it alone
retriever = index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=3)
nodes = retriever.retrieve('退款政策是什么？')   # List[NodeWithScore]
for n in nodes:
    print(round(n.score, 3), n.node.text[:50])
# 注意：此处只检索，尚未生成答案
显式构造 VectorIndexRetriever，逐条查看分数与来源Construct VectorIndexRetriever explicitly to inspect each score and source
from llama_index.core.retrievers import VectorIndexRetriever

# 直接构造检索器（等价于 index.as_retriever，但更显式）
retriever = VectorIndexRetriever(index=index, similarity_top_k=4)
for n in retriever.retrieve('国际订单的退款要多久？'):
    print(f'{n.score:.3f}  {n.node.get_content()[:50]}')
    print('  来源:', n.node.metadata.get('file_name'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Retriever 返回 top-k 个带分数的 Node，不产生最终答案。A Retriever returns the top-k scored Nodes, not the final answer.
  • similarity_top_k 太小漏召回、太大引噪声。Too small a similarity_top_k misses; too large adds noise.
  • 检索与生成解耦，便于单独调试与评估检索质量。Decoupling retrieval from generation lets you debug and evaluate retrieval on its own.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把“取相关片段”独立成 Retriever，意味着你能在不动 LLM 的前提下，专门优化“召回了对的内容没有”这一核心问题。
Isolating “fetch relevant pieces” as a Retriever means you can optimize the core question — “did we recall the right content?” — without ever touching the LLM.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 检索分数普遍偏低。你按什么顺序排查(top_k / embedding / 切块)？每一步怎么用数据验证而不是猜？Retrieval scores are uniformly low. In what order do you investigate (top_k / embedding / chunking), and how do you verify each step with data rather than guessing?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：先看正确块是否进了 top-k——top_k 只改数量不改分，不是第一手。正确块没进→切块太碎/太粗或 embedding 不贴领域(用命中率/MRR 量化、逐一替换变量验证)；进了但分低→query 与 doc 表述差距大(考虑改写/HyDE/rerank)。始终用一组带 gold 块的查询做对照，避免凭感觉。🔑 Key: first check whether the right chunk is even in top-k — top_k changes count, not scores, so it's not the first move. Not there → bad chunking or off-domain embedding (quantify with hit-rate/MRR, swap one variable at a time); there but low → query/doc phrasing gap (consider rewriting/HyDE/rerank). Always compare against a gold-chunk query set, not vibes.
好召回Good recall
top-k 全相关、分数高，正确依据在列——retrieve() 一看便知。top-k all relevant, high scores, the right evidence present — visible from retrieve() alone.
vs
坏召回Bad recall
混入噪声或正确块没进 top-k、分数偏低——问题在检索，不必怪 LLM。noise mixed in or the right chunk missing / low score — the fault is retrieval, not the LLM.
不调用 LLM，只看 retrieve() 的结果就能判断召回好坏Judge recall from retrieve() alone, without ever calling the LLM
🎯 2. 为什么要把检索独立成一等公民？这让你能脱离 LLM 单独做什么评估、有什么工程好处？Why make retrieval a first-class citizen? What can you evaluate without the LLM, and what's the engineering payoff?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：检索与生成解耦后，“召回对不对”可脱离 LLM 单独度量与优化。直接看 retrieve() 的 Node 是否含正确依据，用命中率/MRR 量化；于是调 top_k/embedding/切块都能秒级验证、不必每次跑昂贵生成，两类问题(召回 vs 生成)也不再纠缠。🔑 Key: decoupling retrieval from generation lets you measure and optimize 'is recall right' without the LLM. Inspect whether retrieve()'s Nodes hold the right evidence (hit-rate/MRR), so tuning top_k/embedding/chunking is verified in seconds without paying for generation — and the two problems (recall vs generation) stop entangling.

第三部分 · 查询路径

13 · 节点后处理 Postprocessors

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

检索回来的 Node 在喂给 LLM 之前还能再加工：过滤低分、重排（rerank）把最相关的提前、或替换为句窗上下文。这一步便宜却常常显著提升答案质量。Before the Nodes reach the LLM they can be reworked: filter low scores, rerank the most relevant to the top, or replace them with sentence-window context. It's cheap yet often a big quality win.

检索结果Retrieved
原始 top-k Noderaw top-k Nodes
→
后处理Post-process
过滤 / 重排 / 替换filter / rerank / replace
→
精选 NodeCurated Nodes
→
交给 LLMHand to the LLM
后处理是检索与生成之间的“质检站”：先把 Node 修整好，再送进 LLMPost-processing is a “QC station” between retrieval and generation: groom the Nodes before they reach the LLM
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
取回的资料先筛掉跑题的、把最相关的排到最前，再交给写手——写手只读精选过的几页。
Sift out the off-topic pages, move the most relevant to the front, then hand them to the writer — who only reads the curated few.

常用后处理器Common postprocessors

后处理器Postprocessor做什么What it does
SimilarityPostprocessorSimilarityPostprocessor按 similarity_cutoff 丢掉低分drop nodes below similarity_cutoff
Rerank（LLM / Cohere…）Rerank (LLM / Cohere…)用更强模型重排相关性re-score relevance with a stronger model
MetadataReplacementPostProcessorMetadataReplacementPostProcessor把句窗节点换成 window 上下文swap window-node text for its window
过滤前Before cutoff
问「退款多久到账？」检索 top-k：
0.86 退款到账时限 ✓
0.41 配送时效 ✗ 低分却混进 top-k
→ 答案被带偏：“一般 3–5 个工作日送达”——答成了配送，答非所问。
Ask “How long until a refund lands?”; top-k:
0.86 refund timing ✓
0.41 delivery times ✗ low score, still slips in
→ Answer derails: “usually delivered in 3–5 business days” — that's shipping, off-question.
vs
过滤后After cutoff (0.7)
similarity_cutoff=0.7 丢掉 0.41 那块，只留：
0.86 退款到账时限 ✓
→ 答案命中：“退款 3–5 个工作日原路退回”——同一个问题，这次答对了。
similarity_cutoff=0.7 drops the 0.41 chunk, leaving:
0.86 refund timing ✓
→ Answer lands: “refunds post back to source in 3–5 business days” — same question, now correct.
同一个问题：滤掉一个低分噪声块，答案就从“答非所问”变成“命中正确依据”Same question: drop one low-score noise chunk and the answer flips from off-topic to on-target

最便宜的一档提质The cheapest quality lever

后处理介于“检索之后、生成之前”，多是非 LLM 的轻量操作（打分阈值、重排），却能去掉噪声、补回上下文。因为不重训、不换模型，它往往是 RAG 调优里性价比最高的一步。
Post-processing sits “after retrieval, before generation,” and is mostly lightweight non-LLM work (score thresholds, reranking) that removes noise and restores context. Because it needs no retraining and no model swap, it is often the best bang-for-buck step in RAG tuning.
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
postprocessor/node.py · SimilarityPostprocessor — 相似度阈值过滤similarity-threshold filtering
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
postprocessor/metadata_replacement.py · MetadataReplacementPostProcessor — 配合句窗切块还原上下文restores context for sentence-window chunks
深入：后处理的来龙去脉Deep dive: the ins and outs of post-processing点击展开expand
🧪 示例：一行阈值过滤🧪 Example: a one-line threshold filter
SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7).postprocess_nodes(nodes) 直接返回保留下来的 Node，可对比过滤前后的数量。
SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7).postprocess_nodes(nodes) returns just the kept Nodes; compare the count before and after.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把“检索后、生成前”做成可插拔的一串 postprocessor，你能用最低成本叠加多种提质手段，互不影响。
Modeling “after retrieval, before generation” as a pluggable chain of postprocessors lets you stack several quality boosts at minimal cost, each independent of the others.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
每个后处理器实现 postprocess_nodes(nodes)，输入输出都是 List[NodeWithScore]；SimilarityPostprocessor 把分数低于 cutoff 的直接丢弃。
Each postprocessor implements postprocess_nodes(nodes), taking and returning a List[NodeWithScore]; SimilarityPostprocessor simply drops anything below the cutoff.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
阈值过滤便宜但粗糙；交叉编码器 rerank（如 Cohere / LLM rerank）更准但要额外一次调用——按预算与质量需求取舍。
Threshold filtering is cheap but blunt; cross-encoder reranking (e.g. Cohere / LLM rerank) is more accurate but costs an extra call — trade off by budget and quality needs.
检索与生成之间的“质检站”a QC station between retrieval and generation
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import SimilarityPostprocessor

nodes = index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=5).retrieve('退款政策？')
pp = SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7)
kept = pp.postprocess_nodes(nodes)   # 丢掉分数低于 0.7 的
print(len(nodes), '->', len(kept))

# 句窗专用：把单句节点替换为其上下文窗口
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import MetadataReplacementPostProcessor
mr = MetadataReplacementPostProcessor(target_metadata_key='window')
句窗检索：命中一句，却把整段上下文喂给 LLMSentence-window: match one sentence, feed the LLM its whole window
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceWindowNodeParser
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import MetadataReplacementPostProcessor

# 建索引时按单句切，并把前后句存进 metadata['window']
parser = SentenceWindowNodeParser.from_defaults(
    window_size=3, window_metadata_key='window',
    original_text_metadata_key='original')

# 查询时把命中的单句节点，还原成它的上下文窗口再交给 LLM
engine = index.as_query_engine(
    similarity_top_k=3,
    node_postprocessors=[MetadataReplacementPostProcessor(target_metadata_key='window')],
)
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 后处理在检索之后、生成之前，调整喂给 LLM 的 Node。Postprocessing sits after retrieval, before generation, shaping the Nodes the LLM sees.
  • similarity_cutoff 滤噪；rerank 提相关性；窗口替换补上下文。similarity_cutoff denoises; rerank lifts relevance; window replacement restores context.
  • 它便宜（多为非 LLM 或一次轻量调用）却常带来明显提升。It's cheap (often non-LLM or one light call) yet frequently a clear win.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把“检索后、生成前”抽象成一串可插拔 postprocessor，让你在不重训、不换模型的情况下，用最低成本提升答案质量——RAG 调优性价比最高的一环。
Modeling “after retrieval, before generation” as pluggable postprocessors lets you raise answer quality at the lowest cost — no retraining, no model swap. The best bang-for-buck in RAG tuning.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7) 的作用是？What does SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7) do?
  1. 重新向量化Re-embed everything
  2. 只取前 0.7 个 NodeKeep only the first 0.7 Nodes
  3. 把所有分数提高到 0.7Raise every score to 0.7
  4. 丢弃相似度低于 0.7 的 NodeDrop Nodes with similarity below 0.7
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：DAnswer: D 它按阈值过滤掉低相关 Node，减少噪声进入生成阶段。It filters out low-relevance Nodes by threshold, reducing noise before generation.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你想用最低成本提升答案质量。为什么后处理是性价比最高的一环？similarity_cutoff 怎么定？怎么证明它真的提升了——要看“答案”而不只是节点数？You want the cheapest quality lift. Why is post-processing the best bang-for-buck, how do you set similarity_cutoff, and how do you prove it actually helped — looking at answers, not just node counts?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：后处理在“检索后/生成前”，多为非 LLM 的轻量操作，不重训不换模型就能去噪提质。similarity_cutoff 看相关/不相关块的分数分布、卡在两者之间的谷，且分数尺度因 embedding 而异、要按模型重标。证明：同一组问题比较答案的 Faithfulness/正确率 before vs after，而不是只看“过滤掉几个节点”。🔑 Key: post-processing sits after retrieval / before generation, mostly lightweight non-LLM work that denoises and lifts quality with no retraining or model swap. Set similarity_cutoff from the score distribution of relevant vs irrelevant chunks (the valley between them); scales differ per embedding, so re-calibrate. Prove it by comparing answer Faithfulness/correctness before vs after on a fixed set — not just 'how many nodes got dropped'.
过滤前Before cutoff
混入“配送时效”低分块 → 答案被带偏、答非所问。a low-score 'shipping' chunk slips in → the answer drifts off-topic.
vs
过滤后After cutoff
只剩“退款”高分块 → 答案正确、切题。only the high-score 'refund' chunk remains → the answer is correct.
看答案的 before/after，才能坐实“显著提升”的主张Compare answers before/after to substantiate the 'big lift' claim
🎯 2. 阈值过滤 vs 交叉编码器 rerank 分别什么时候用？句窗 + MetadataReplacementPostProcessor 解决什么矛盾？When do you use threshold filtering vs cross-encoder reranking, and what tension do sentence-window + MetadataReplacementPostProcessor resolve?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：阈值便宜但粗糙(先砍明显低分)；rerank 准但贵一次调用(用更强模型纠正向量排序)。常组合：多取→cutoff→rerank。句窗+替换解决“检索要精准(小块) vs 生成要上下文(大块)”的矛盾：单句检索保证精准，命中后替换成前后句的 window 再喂 LLM——检索粒度与喂入粒度解耦。🔑 Key: thresholds are cheap but blunt (cut obvious low scores); reranking is accurate but costs an extra call (a stronger model fixes vector ordering). Often combined: fetch wide → cutoff → rerank. Sentence-window + replacement resolves 'retrieve precisely (small) vs generate with context (large)': retrieve single sentences for precision, then replace with the surrounding window before generation — decoupling retrieval granularity from what the LLM reads.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 相似度阈值设太高会怎样、太低又会怎样？你会用什么信号来定这个阈值？What happens if the similarity cutoff is too high vs too low — and what signal would you use to set it?
第三部分 · 查询路径

14 · 响应合成 Response Synthesizers

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

拿到（过滤/重排后的）top-k Node，怎么揉成一个答案？Response Synthesizer 决定“多个片段→单个回答”的策略，核心是应对上下文窗口与片段数量的权衡。Given the (filtered/reranked) top-k Nodes, how do you fuse them into one answer? The Response Synthesizer sets the “many chunks → one answer” strategy — chiefly trading off context window against number of chunks.

模式Mode
形态：多个片段如何变成一个答案Shape: how many chunks become one answer
compact（默认）compact (default)
尽量塞满上下文，一次写完pack the context, write once
refinerefine
逐块链式精炼，答案不断被改写chain through chunks, refining the answer each step
tree_summarizetree_summarize
分组总结，再把总结向上合并summarize in groups, then merge summaries upward
accumulateaccumulate
每块各自作答，最后汇总answer each chunk separately, then collect
四种 ResponseMode 的“形态”速览The four ResponseModes at a glance, by shape
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
写手拿到几页资料的几种写法：逐页精炼（refine）、塞满一次写（compact）、分组总结再合并（tree_summarize）、每页各答再汇总（accumulate）。
Different ways a writer drafts from several pages: refine page by page, pack as many as fit and write once (compact), summarize in groups then merge (tree_summarize), or answer each page then collect (accumulate).

常用 ResponseModeCommon ResponseModes

模式Mode适合Good for
compact（默认）compact (default)通用、省调用general, fewer calls
refinerefine片段多、需细读many chunks, careful reading
tree_summarizetree_summarize总结类问题summary questions
accumulateaccumulate逐条抽取per-chunk extraction

多片段如何收敛成一个答案How many chunks converge into one answer

合成的核心矛盾是：检索到的片段可能装不进一次上下文窗口。compact 尽量塞、少调用；refine 逐块迭代、读得细；tree_summarize 分层合并、擅长全局总结。选 mode 本质上是在“上下文窗口”和“片段数量”之间取舍。
The core tension of synthesis: the retrieved chunks may not fit in one context window. compact packs them and minimizes calls; refine iterates chunk by chunk and reads carefully; tree_summarize merges in layers and excels at global summaries. Choosing a mode is fundamentally a trade-off between context window and number of chunks.
8 个检索片段8 retrieved chunks太多，装不进一次上下文too many for a single context window
↓
分组各自总结summarize each group→ 几个小结→ a few partial summaries
↓
再总结这些小结summarize those summaries→ 更少的中间结果→ fewer intermediate results
↓
单个最终答案one final answer
tree_summarize：像锦标赛一样逐层向上合并tree_summarize: merge upward, round by round, like a tournament
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
response_synthesizers/factory.py · get_response_synthesizer — 按 ResponseMode 造合成器builds a synthesizer for a ResponseMode
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
response_synthesizers/type.py · ResponseMode — 所有合成策略的枚举the enum of synthesis strategies
深入：响应合成的取舍Deep dive: the trade-offs of response synthesis点击展开expand
🧪 示例：显式造合成器🧪 Example: build a synthesizer explicitly
get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='tree_summarize') 造出的合成器可单独使用，也可传给 query engine，便于精确控制合成策略。
get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='tree_summarize') builds a synthesizer you can use on its own or pass to a query engine, for precise control over the synthesis strategy.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把“拼接片段”抽象成可切换的 ResponseMode，让同一套检索结果既能服务精确问答，也能服务全局总结，无需改检索。
Abstracting “stitch the chunks” into switchable ResponseModes lets one set of retrieved results serve both precise Q&A and global summarization — with no change to retrieval.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
ResponseMode 是个枚举；compact 实际是 compact_and_refine——先把片段尽量塞满，装不下时再退回 refine 的逐块迭代。
ResponseMode is an enum; compact is really compact_and_refine — pack chunks first, falling back to refine's chunk-by-chunk iteration when they don't all fit.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
通用问答用 compact（省调用）；要细读多片段用 refine；要全局总结用 tree_summarize；要逐条抽取用 accumulate。
Use compact for general Q&A (fewer calls), refine to read many chunks carefully, tree_summarize for global summaries, and accumulate for per-chunk extraction.
选 mode = 选“多片段→单答案”的策略choosing a mode = choosing the many→one strategy
from llama_index.core import get_response_synthesizer

# 方式一：直接在 query engine 上选模式
engine = index.as_query_engine(response_mode='tree_summarize')
print(engine.query('把这些文档总结成 3 点'))

# 方式二：显式造一个合成器（便于自定义装配，见下一课）
synth = get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='compact')
显式装配合成器：把 refine 接到查询引擎上Wire a synthesizer explicitly: attach refine to the query engine
from llama_index.core import get_response_synthesizer

# 显式造一个 refine 合成器，逐块迭代精炼答案
synth = get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='refine')

# 装到 query engine 上：检索照旧，合成改用 refine
engine = index.as_query_engine(response_synthesizer=synth, similarity_top_k=6)
print(engine.query('把这几篇文档的结论逐点对比一下'))

把三课串成一条查询路径Threading lessons 12–14 into one query path

第 12、13、14 课各自从 index.as_retriever 起步，读起来像三段彼此独立的代码。其实一次 .query() 就把它们串成一条流水线：同一批 Node 被检索取回、被后处理筛选、再交合成器落笔，一路传递下去。
Lessons 12, 13 and 14 each start over at index.as_retriever, so they read like three disconnected snippets. In reality one .query() threads them into a single pipeline: the same batch of Nodes is retrieved, filtered by post-processing, then handed to the synthesizer — flowing straight through.

一个问题一路传递：第 12 课取回 → 第 13 课筛 → 第 14 课合成One question passed straight through: Lesson 12 retrieves → Lesson 13 filters → Lesson 14 synthesizes
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Synthesizer 解决“多个 Node 如何合成一个答案”。The synthesizer solves “how many Nodes become one answer”.
  • compact 省调用，tree_summarize 擅总结，refine 重细读。compact saves calls, tree_summarize summarizes, refine reads carefully.
  • 模式选择本质是上下文窗口 vs 片段数量的权衡。Mode choice is fundamentally context window vs number of chunks.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
把“拼接片段”这件容易写死的事抽象成可切换的 ResponseMode，让同一套检索结果能服务“精确问答”到“全局总结”不同需求。
Abstracting “stitch the chunks” into switchable ResponseModes lets one set of retrieved results serve everything from precise Q&A to global summarization.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 片段很多但上下文窗口很小。你怎么选 ResponseMode？compact 和 refine 的代价对比？怎么验证选对了？Many chunks but a small context window. How do you choose a ResponseMode, what's the cost difference between compact and refine, and how do you verify you chose right?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：选 mode 是“上下文窗口 vs 片段数量”的取舍——窗口小+片段多时矛盾最尖锐。refine 对每片段各调一次 LLM(多/慢/贵，但都读到)；compact 尽量合并(调用少，但小窗能塞的有限、可能漏或频繁退化为 refine)。验证：比较各 mode 的答案质量(Faithfulness/完整度)与成本/延迟，按预算取平衡。🔑 Key: choosing a mode trades context window against number of chunks — the tension peaks with a small window and many chunks. refine calls the LLM once per chunk (more/slower/costly, but reads all); compact merges to cut calls (but a small window limits what fits, risking misses or falling back to refine). Verify by comparing each mode's answer quality (Faithfulness/completeness) and cost/latency, balancing to budget.
🎯 2. “多片段→单答案”的核心矛盾是什么？compact 实际是什么、为什么把它做默认？What's the core tension of 'many chunks → one answer', what is compact really, and why is it the default?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：核心矛盾是检索片段可能装不进一次上下文窗口。compact 其实是 compact_and_refine：先把尽量多的片段塞满一个 prompt(减少调用)，装不下时再退回 refine 逐块迭代——兼顾省钱与不丢信息，所以适合做通用默认。🔑 Key: the core tension is that retrieved chunks may not fit in one context window. compact is really compact_and_refine: pack as many chunks as fit into one prompt (fewer calls), falling back to refine's chunk-by-chunk iteration when they don't — balancing cost and completeness, which makes it a sensible default.
🎯 3. 你要“把整库逐点总结成一页纪要”。你选哪个 mode、为什么不是 compact？You must 'summarize the whole base into a one-page brief'. Which mode, and why not compact?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 tree_summarize——它要求看“全部”内容、分组逐层合并，正合“全局总结”。compact 以“尽量塞满+少调用”为目标，面对超出窗口的大量片段会塞不下、易漏；总结类问题宁可多调用也要覆盖全。🔑 Key: use tree_summarize — it sees all content and merges in layers, exactly fitting a global summary. compact aims to pack-and-minimize-calls and, with chunks exceeding the window, can't fit everything and risks missing parts; for summaries you'd rather pay more calls to cover all.

第三部分 · 查询路径

15 · 查询引擎 Query Engine

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

QueryEngine 把检索器 + 后处理 + 响应合成器装配成一个 .query() 入口。index.as_query_engine() 是快捷方式；RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...) 让你自由拼装。A QueryEngine assembles retriever + postprocessors + synthesizer behind one .query() call. index.as_query_engine() is the shortcut; RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...) lets you wire it by hand.

检索器Retriever
取 top-kfetch top-k
→
后处理器Postprocessors
过滤 / 重排filter / rerank
→
合成器Synthesizer
多片段→单答案many → one
→
.query().query()
一个入口one entry
QueryEngine = 把三个正交组件装配进一个 .query() 入口A QueryEngine wires three orthogonal components behind one .query() call
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
把“图书管理员（检索）+ 质检（后处理）+ 写手（合成）”组装成一个一键问答窗口。
Bundle “librarian (retrieve) + QC (postprocess) + writer (synthesize)” into a single one-click Q&A window.

两种装配方式Two ways to assemble

方式Way适合Good for
index.as_query_engine(...)index.as_query_engine(...)快速、默认装配fast, default wiring
RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...)RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...)自定义检索器/后处理/合成器custom retriever/postproc/synth

QueryEngine 是查询路径的组合根The QueryEngine is the query path's composition root

检索器、后处理器、合成器是三个正交的组件：换检索器不影响合成策略，加后处理器不影响检索。QueryEngine 只负责把它们装配起来、对外暴露一个 .query()。值得记住的是：index.as_query_engine(...) 与 RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...) 产出的其实是同一种 QueryEngine，只是装配深度不同——前者用默认接线、一行起步，后者让你逐件指定检索器 / 后处理器 / 合成器。
The retriever, postprocessors and synthesizer are three orthogonal components: swapping the retriever doesn't touch the synthesis strategy, and adding a postprocessor doesn't touch retrieval. The QueryEngine just wires them together behind one .query(). Worth remembering: index.as_query_engine(...) and RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(...) yield the very same kind of QueryEngine — they differ only in wiring depth: the former starts in one line with default wiring, the latter lets you specify the retriever / postprocessors / synthesizer piece by piece.
engine.query('…')engine.query('…')收到问题receives the question
↓
retrieve()retrieve()→ top-k NodeWithScore→ top-k NodeWithScore
↓
postprocesspostprocess→ 过滤/重排后的 Node→ filtered/reranked Nodes
↓
synthesize()synthesize()→ 交 LLM 据此作答→ LLM answers from them
↓
ResponseResponseanswer + source_nodesanswer + source_nodes
一次 query 的内部时序the internal timeline of a single query

🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
base/base_query_engine.py · BaseQueryEngine.query — 查询路径的统一入口the unified query entry point
深入：查询引擎的装配Deep dive: assembling the query engine点击展开expand
🧪 示例：手装三件套🧪 Example: wire the three parts by hand
RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(retriever=…, node_postprocessors=[…], response_synthesizer=…) 让你逐件指定，组合出非默认的行为。
RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(retriever=…, node_postprocessors=[…], response_synthesizer=…) lets you specify each part to compose non-default behavior.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
组合根模式把“装配”与“组件”分离：组件各自演进，装配方式保持稳定，于是定制 RAG 不必重写每一站。
The composition-root pattern separates “wiring” from “components”: components evolve on their own while the wiring stays stable, so customizing RAG never means rewriting every stop.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
BaseQueryEngine.query() 内部调 _query()，后者先 retrieve() 取 Node、过一遍后处理，再 synthesize() 生成 Response。
BaseQueryEngine.query() calls _query(), which first retrieve()s Nodes, runs them through postprocessing, then synthesize()s the Response.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
那什么时候才真的需要 from_args(...)？当你要换非默认检索器（如 BM25 / 混合检索）、串联多个后处理器，或指定特定 ResponseMode 时——否则 as_query_engine(...) 的默认装配已经够用。
So when do you actually reach for from_args(...)? When you need a non-default retriever (e.g. BM25 / hybrid), a chain of postprocessors, or a specific ResponseMode — otherwise the default wiring of as_query_engine(...) already suffices.
QueryEngine = 查询路径的“组合根”the QueryEngine is the query path's composition root
from llama_index.core.query_engine import RetrieverQueryEngine
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import SimilarityPostprocessor
from llama_index.core import get_response_synthesizer

# 手动拼装：检索器 + 后处理 + 合成器
engine = RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(
    retriever=index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=5),
    node_postprocessors=[SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.7)],
    response_synthesizer=get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='compact'),
)
resp = engine.query('退款政策是什么？')
print(resp, '\n依据:', [n.node_id for n in resp.source_nodes])
as_query_engine 一行定制：换 prompt 与 top_k，无需手装Customize in one line with as_query_engine: swap prompt and top_k, no hand-wiring
from llama_index.core import PromptTemplate

qa = PromptTemplate(
    '仅根据下面的资料回答；若资料不足就说不知道。\n'
    '资料：{context_str}\n问题：{query_str}\n答案：')

# 一行定制：自定义 prompt + top_k（对照上面的 from_args 手装）
engine = index.as_query_engine(text_qa_template=qa, similarity_top_k=4)
print(engine.query('退款政策是什么？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • QueryEngine 串起检索→后处理→合成，对外只暴露 .query()。A QueryEngine chains retrieve→postprocess→synthesize, exposing only .query().
  • 三件套可独立替换，组合出不同行为。Each of the three parts is independently swappable.
  • response.source_nodes 保留可溯源的依据。response.source_nodes keeps the traceable evidence.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
QueryEngine 是查询路径的组合根：把三个正交组件组装起来。理解它，你就能把“默认问答”改造成任意 RAG 变体。
The QueryEngine is the query path's composition root: it assembles three orthogonal components. Grasp it and you can reshape “default Q&A” into any RAG variant.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要把 demo 问答升级成“只引用、不编造、可灰度替换检索策略”的客服引擎。你会怎么用 QueryEngine 装配？为什么拆成三件而不是写死一个函数？怎么验证改造没把效果搞差？You're upgrading demo Q&A into a support engine that is cite-only, never-invent, with swappable retrieval. How do you assemble it via the QueryEngine, why split into three parts instead of one hard-coded function, and how do you verify the rebuild didn't regress?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：QueryEngine 是“组合根”，把检索器/后处理/合成器三件正交组件装在一起，可独立替换。拆三件→换检索器不影响合成、加后处理不影响检索，灰度某一件不动其余；写死一个函数则牵一发动全身。装配：retriever + [cutoff/rerank] + 严格 text_qa_template(只引用/给出处)。验证：用回归集比较改造前后的 Faithfulness/正确率，确认没退化再上。🔑 Key: the QueryEngine is a composition root assembling three orthogonal parts — retriever / postprocessors / synthesizer — each independently swappable. Splitting them means swapping the retriever doesn't touch synthesis and adding postprocessing doesn't touch retrieval, so you can canary one part; a hard-coded function couples everything. Assemble retriever + [cutoff/rerank] + a strict text_qa_template (cite-only). Verify with a regression set comparing Faithfulness/correctness before vs after, shipping only on no regression.
🎯 2. 什么时候从 as_query_engine 下沉到 from_args？这个取舍你怎么向团队解释？When do you drop from as_query_engine to from_args, and how do you explain the trade-off to your team?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：二者产出同一种 QueryEngine，只是装配深度不同——默认够用就用快捷方式，要定制某一站才下沉。向团队解释：as_query_engine 一行起步、维护省心；from_args 给最大控制力(自定义 retriever/后处理/合成/prompt)。规范：默认走快捷方式，确有定制需求再下沉，避免无谓的样板。🔑 Key: both yield the same QueryEngine, differing only in wiring depth — use the shortcut when defaults suffice, drop down to customize a stop. Explain it as: as_query_engine is one-line and low-maintenance; from_args gives maximum control (custom retriever/postproc/synth/prompt). Convention: default to the shortcut, drop down only on a real customization need, avoiding needless boilerplate.
🎯 3. 一次 .query() 内部时序是什么、为什么是这个顺序？What's the internal sequence of one .query(), and why this order?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：retrieve() 取 top-k → node_postprocessors 过滤/重排/替换 → synthesize() 合成 → Response(answer + source_nodes)。顺序有因：必须先取回候选才能后处理，必须先精选再合成(否则把噪声喂给 LLM)；source_nodes 一路保留，保证答案可溯源。🔑 Key: retrieve() fetches top-k → node_postprocessors filter/rerank/replace → synthesize() fuses → Response (answer + source_nodes). The order is principled: you must fetch candidates before post-processing them, and curate before synthesis (else you feed the LLM noise); source_nodes are carried throughout to keep the answer traceable.

  • 要把“默认问答”改造成“只引用、不编造”的客服引擎，你会替换 QueryEngine 的哪几件组件？To reshape default Q&A into a 'cite-only, never invent' support engine, which components of the QueryEngine would you swap?
第三部分 · 查询路径

16 · 聊天引擎 Chat Engine

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

ChatEngine 在 QueryEngine 之上加多轮记忆。两种范式：condense_question（把对话历史压成一个独立问题再检索）和 context（每轮都检索并把片段注入上下文）。A ChatEngine adds multi-turn memory on top of a QueryEngine. Two paradigms: condense_question (condense the history into one standalone question, then retrieve) and context (retrieve every turn and inject the snippets into context).

condense_questioncondense_question
先把“对话历史 + 新问题”压成一个独立问题，再用它检索。指代先消解，检索更准。
First condense “history + new question” into one standalone question, then retrieve with it. Coreference is resolved first, so retrieval is sharper.
vs
contextcontext
每一轮都直接检索，把命中的片段注入系统上下文，连同历史一起交给 LLM。
Every turn retrieves directly and injects the hit snippets into the system context, handed to the LLM along with the history.
两种多轮范式：先压缩问题，还是每轮注入上下文Two multi-turn paradigms: condense the question first, or inject context each turn
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
QueryEngine 像一次性问答台；ChatEngine 像记得前文的客服，能听懂“那它的退款呢？”里的“它”。
A QueryEngine is a one-shot help desk; a ChatEngine is a support agent who remembers the thread and understands what “it” refers to in “and its refund?”.

三种聊天模式Three chat modes

ChatModeChatMode怎么处理多轮How it handles turns
condense_questioncondense_question历史+新问 → 独立问题 → 检索history+new → standalone question → retrieve
contextcontext每轮检索，片段注入系统上下文retrieve each turn, inject as context
condense_plus_contextcondense_plus_context先压缩问题，再检索注入（两者结合）condense then retrieve+inject (both)

多轮的真正难点What's actually hard about multi-turn

多轮聊天不是给 QueryEngine 套个循环就行。难点有二：一是指代消解——“它 / 那 / 上面说的”要先还原成具体所指；二是用哪个问题去检索——是拿用户这轮的原话，还是拿指代消解后补全的独立问题？两种 ChatMode 正是这第二个问题的两种答案：condense_question 先把“历史 + 新问”压成一个独立问题、再用它检索；context 直接用原话每轮检索、把片段注入上下文。注意：两种模式都每轮检索——真正“要不要检索”的按需判断属于 Agent / Router 的范畴（见第 18 课）。
Multi-turn chat is not just wrapping a loop around a QueryEngine. Two things are hard: coreference — “it / that / the one above” must be resolved to a concrete referent first; and which question to retrieve with — the user's raw words this turn, or the standalone question rebuilt after resolving the coreference? The two ChatModes are two answers to this second problem: condense_question first condenses “history + new question” into one standalone query, then retrieves with it; context retrieves every turn with the raw words and injects the snippets. Note: both modes retrieve on every turn — truly deciding whether to retrieve at all is agent / router behavior (Lesson 18).

多轮的关键：先把“它 / 那”解析成具体所指，再检索作答，并记住本轮The crux of multi-turn: resolve “it / that” to a concrete referent, then retrieve, answer, and remember the turn

深入：多轮 RAG 的机制Deep dive: the mechanics of multi-turn RAG点击展开expand
🧪 示例：连问两轮🧪 Example: two chained turns
chat.chat('退款政策？') 后再 chat.chat('那国际订单呢？')，引擎会用上一轮把“那”消解成“国际订单的退款”，再检索作答。
After chat.chat('refund policy?'), a follow-up chat.chat('and intl orders?') uses the prior turn to resolve “and …” into “refund for intl orders,” then retrieves and answers.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
因为多轮的难点不在“记历史”，而在“理解依赖历史的新问题”。把指代消解与检索时机显式化，聊天才会稳。
Because the hard part of multi-turn isn't “storing history,” it's “understanding a new question that depends on it.” Making coreference and retrieval-timing explicit is what makes chat robust.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
CondenseQuestionChatEngine 先用 LLM 把历史+新问压成独立问题再检索；ContextChatEngine 每轮检索并把片段塞进 system 提示。
CondenseQuestionChatEngine first uses the LLM to condense history+question into a standalone query, then retrieves; ContextChatEngine retrieves each turn and stuffs the snippets into the system prompt.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
condense_plus_context 兼顾两者——先压缩问题、再检索注入，通用性最好，是大多数客服 / 问答助手的默认选择。
condense_plus_context combines both — condense the question, then retrieve and inject — the most general option and the default for most support / Q&A assistants.
多轮 RAG = 指代消解 + 每轮检索multi-turn RAG = coreference + retrieval each turn
chat = index.as_chat_engine(chat_mode='condense_plus_context')
print(chat.chat('你们的退款政策是什么？'))
print(chat.chat('那国际订单也一样吗？'))   # ‘那/也’ 依赖上一轮，引擎会消解指代

chat.reset()   # 清空多轮记忆
显式装配 ContextChatEngine：自带记忆与系统提示Wire ContextChatEngine explicitly: with its own memory and system prompt
from llama_index.core.chat_engine import ContextChatEngine
from llama_index.core.memory import ChatMemoryBuffer

memory = ChatMemoryBuffer.from_defaults(token_limit=3000)
chat = ContextChatEngine.from_defaults(
    retriever=index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=3),
    memory=memory,
    system_prompt='你是一名严谨的客服，只依据检索到的资料回答。',
)
print(chat.chat('你们支持哪些支付方式？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • ChatEngine = QueryEngine + 记忆，支持指代消解的多轮问答。ChatEngine = QueryEngine + memory, enabling coreference-aware multi-turn Q&A.
  • condense_question 重写问题；context 每轮注入检索片段。condense_question rewrites the question; context injects retrieved snippets each turn.
  • condense_plus_context 兼顾两者，通用性最好。condense_plus_context combines both and is the most general.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
多轮 RAG 的真正难点是指代消解，以及用哪个问题去检索——用原话，还是用消解后补全的独立问题。两种 mode 给出两种答案（且都每轮检索）——这也是为什么聊天不只是“给 QueryEngine 套个循环”。
The real challenge of multi-turn RAG is coreference and which question to retrieve with — the raw words, or the standalone question rebuilt after resolving it. The two modes give two answers (both retrieving every turn) — which is why chat is more than “wrap a loop around a QueryEngine.”

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 多轮对话里用户问“那它呢？”，condense_question 模式怎么处理？In a multi-turn chat the user asks “and what about it?” — how does condense_question mode handle it?
  1. 只用关键词匹配Use keyword matching only
  2. 先把对话历史+新问压成一个独立完整问题，再检索First condense history + new question into one standalone question, then retrieve
  3. 直接拿“那它呢”去检索Retrieve directly with “and what about it?”
  4. 忽略对话历史Ignore the chat history
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B condense 模式先把指代消解成一个独立问题，确保检索到正确片段。Condense mode resolves the reference into a standalone question first, so retrieval finds the right chunks.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要做多轮客服。两个真正的难点是什么？condense_question 和 context 都每轮检索吗？“要不要检索”由谁决定？你会选哪种 mode、怎么验证多轮效果？You're building multi-turn support. What are the two real hard parts? Do condense_question and context both retrieve every turn? Who decides 'whether to retrieve'? Which mode would you pick, and how do you evaluate multi-turn quality?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：难点是“指代消解 + 用哪个问题去检索”；两种 mode 都每轮检索，“要不要检索”是 agent/router 的事，不是这两个 mode。选择：condense_plus_context 通用性最好(先消解再检索注入)。验证：用多轮对话集，看带指代的追问是否被正确消解、答案是否仍忠于检索——单轮指标不够。🔑 Key: the hard parts are coreference + which question to retrieve with; both modes retrieve every turn, and deciding 'whether to retrieve' is agent/router territory, not these modes. Pick condense_plus_context as the most general (condense, then retrieve + inject). Evaluate with a multi-turn dialogue set, checking whether pronoun-laden follow-ups resolve correctly and answers stay grounded — single-turn metrics aren't enough.

🎯 2. 用户追问“那国际订单呢”被解析错、检索跑偏。你怎么排查和改善？On 'and intl orders?', the engine resolves it wrong and retrieval derails. How do you debug and improve it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：先打印 condense 之后生成的“独立问题”——很多实现可看改写后的 query。若改写错→优化 condense 的 prompt、保留更多对话历史、或换 condense_plus_context；指代实在复杂时，上 agent 做更强的对话状态管理，或在 UI 端引导用户把指代说明确。🔑 Key: first print the standalone question produced after condensing — many implementations expose the rewritten query. If the rewrite is wrong → improve the condense prompt, keep more history, or switch to condense_plus_context; for genuinely hard references, move to an agent with stronger dialogue-state management, or guide users to disambiguate in the UI.

第四部分 · 进阶

17 · 全局配置 Settings 与 Prompt

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

Settings 是全局默认配置（llm / embed_model / node_parser / chunk_size…），取代了旧的 ServiceContext。Prompt 模板则控制“到底怎么问 LLM”，可按领域定制语气与约束。Settings holds global defaults (llm / embed_model / node_parser / chunk_size…), replacing the old ServiceContext. Prompt templates control “how exactly we ask the LLM”, customizable per domain for tone and constraints.

🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
Settings 像项目的默认设置面板：定一次，处处生效，单处仍可覆盖。Prompt 模板像填空式提问公式，把检索到的上下文和用户问题填进固定结构。
Settings is the project's defaults panel: set once, applies everywhere, still overridable locally. A prompt template is a fill-in-the-blank question form that slots the retrieved context and the user's question into a fixed structure.

Settings 常用项 + Prompt 占位符Common Settings + prompt placeholders

项 / 占位符Item / placeholder含义Meaning
Settings.llmSettings.llm默认生成模型default generation model
Settings.embed_modelSettings.embed_model默认向量化模型default embedding model
Settings.chunk_sizeSettings.chunk_size默认切块大小default chunk size
{context_str} / {query_str}{context_str} / {query_str}Prompt 里填入检索上下文 / 用户问题where context / question are injected
PromptTemplate（问答模板）PromptTemplate (the QA template)
{context_str}{context_str}
检索到的片段在此注入——答案的“依据”retrieved snippets are injected here — the answer's evidence
{query_str}{query_str}
用户问题在此注入——要回答的“题目”the user's question is injected here — the task to answer
固定指令Fixed instructions
语气、边界、“无据就说不知道”等约束写死在模板里tone, limits and rules like “say you don't know” live in the template
Prompt 模板是一张填空卷：两个占位符到运行时才被真实内容填满A prompt template is a fill-in-the-blank form: both placeholders are filled with real content only at run time

全局默认 + 局部覆盖；Prompt 决定“最后一公里”Global defaults + local overrides; the prompt owns the “last mile”

Settings 给全管道一份默认值，省去到处传配置对象；但任何一处都能在构造时就地覆盖，不影响全局。检索决定“拿到哪些上下文”，Prompt 决定“拿同一份上下文怎么问”——检索结果一字不变，换一个语气、约束或输出格式的模板，答案就大不相同。这一步正是 RAG 的“最后一公里”。
Settings hands the whole pipeline a set of defaults, sparing you from threading a config object everywhere; yet any call site can override locally at construction without touching the global. Retrieval decides “which context you get”; the prompt decides “how to ask with that same context” — with identical retrieved snippets, swapping the template's tone, constraints or output format yields a very different answer. That step is RAG's “last mile”.
全局 Settings（基线）Global Settings (baseline)
一处设定，llm / embed_model / chunk_size 成为全管道默认，适合统一基线。
Set once and llm / embed_model / chunk_size become pipeline-wide defaults — ideal for a uniform baseline.
vs
局部覆盖（特例）Local override (special case)
构造某个组件时显式传参，如 as_query_engine(llm=…, text_qa_template=…)，只改这一处而不动全局。
Pass arguments explicitly when building one component, e.g. as_query_engine(llm=…, text_qa_template=…) — changes this spot only, leaving the global intact.
同一套 RAG：全局定基线，局部按需特例化One RAG setup: set a global baseline, then special-case locally on demand
Prompt A · 宽松Prompt A · loose
模板只说“根据资料回答”。检索到的同一份上下文里其实没提保修期，宽松的措辞却纵容 LLM 顺嘴补一句“一般为一年”——看似贴心，实为编造、无出处。
The template merely says “answer from the materials”. The retrieved context never actually mentions the warranty period, yet the loose wording lets the LLM blurt out “usually one year” — helpful-looking, but fabricated and unsourced.
vs
Prompt B · 严格Prompt B · strict
模板写死“只用资料回答；未提及就说‘资料未提及’”。检索结果一字未变、问题也一样，这次 LLM 老实回答“资料未提及”——不编、可追溯。
The template hard-codes “answer only from the materials; if not mentioned, say ‘not in the materials’”. With the retrieved snippets byte-for-byte identical and the same question, the LLM now honestly says “not in the materials” — no fabrication, fully traceable.
同一份上下文、同一个问题，只换 Prompt：答案从“编造”翻转为“老实说不知道”——这就是 RAG 的最后一公里Same context, same question, only the prompt changes: the answer flips from fabrication to an honest “I don't know” — RAG's last mile
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
settings.py · Settings — 全局配置单例（取代 ServiceContext）the global config singleton (replaces ServiceContext)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
prompts/base.py · PromptTemplate — 提示词模板the prompt template type
深入：全局配置与 Prompt 模板Deep dive: global config and prompt templates点击展开expand
🧪 示例：设默认 + 定制模板🧪 Example: set defaults + a custom template
Settings.llm = OpenAI(...) 与 Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(...) 设好全局默认；再用 PromptTemplate('…{context_str}…{query_str}…') 为某个 query engine 定制问答语气与约束。
Settings.llm = OpenAI(...) and Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(...) set the global defaults; then a PromptTemplate('…{context_str}…{query_str}…') customizes the answering tone and constraints for a given query engine.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
全局默认去样板：不必把 llm / embed_model 一路当参数传给每个组件；把 Prompt 显式成模板，则让“最后一公里”的措辞集中、可审、可版本化，而不是散落在代码里的隐式字符串。
Global defaults kill boilerplate: you no longer thread llm / embed_model as arguments into every component. Making the prompt an explicit template keeps the “last-mile” wording centralized, auditable and versionable instead of buried as implicit strings.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
Settings 是一个进程内单例（_Settings）；组件构造时若没收到显式参数，就回退到它的字段。问答模板（text_qa_template）最终流向响应合成器，在合成阶段用检索到的上下文填满占位符，再交给 LLM。
Settings is an in-process singleton (_Settings); when a component is built without explicit arguments, it falls back to these fields. The QA template (text_qa_template) ultimately flows into the response synthesizer, which fills the placeholders with retrieved context at synthesis time before calling the LLM.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
想要全局一致就用 Settings；只想在某一处用不同模型或模板，就在构造时局部传参（如 as_query_engine(llm=…, text_qa_template=…)），覆盖全局而不污染其它链路。
Use Settings for global consistency; when only one spot needs a different model or template, pass it locally at construction (e.g. as_query_engine(llm=…, text_qa_template=…)), overriding the global without polluting other paths.
全局配一次 + 局部定制 Promptconfigure globally + customize the prompt locally
from llama_index.core import Settings, PromptTemplate
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAI

Settings.llm = OpenAI(model='gpt-4o-mini')   # 全局默认，一处生效
Settings.chunk_size = 512

qa = PromptTemplate(
    '只根据下面的上下文回答，未提及就说不知道，不要编造。\n'
    '上下文:\n{context_str}\n问题: {query_str}\n答案: '
)
engine = index.as_query_engine(text_qa_template=qa)   # 定制问答 Prompt
print(engine.query('退款政策？'))
局部覆盖：换掉这一处的 llm 与模板，全局 Settings 原封不动Local override: swap this engine's llm and template; global Settings untouched
from llama_index.core import PromptTemplate
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAI

# 全局 Settings 保持不变；只在这个 query engine 上局部覆盖
strict = PromptTemplate(
    '只依据下面的上下文回答；若上下文未提及，请回答“资料中未提及”。\n'
    '上下文:\n{context_str}\n问题: {query_str}\n答案: '
)
engine = index.as_query_engine(
    llm=OpenAI(model='gpt-4o', temperature=0),   # 这一处换更强的模型
    text_qa_template=strict,                     # 这一处换更严格的模板
)
print(engine.query('保修期是多久？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • Settings 取代 ServiceContext，集中管理默认 llm/embed/切块等。Settings replaces ServiceContext, centralizing default llm/embed/chunking.
  • Prompt 模板用 {context_str} / {query_str} 注入上下文与问题。Prompt templates inject context and question via {context_str} / {query_str}.
  • 全局默认 + 局部覆盖：既省事又灵活。Global defaults + local overrides: convenient yet flexible.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
“全局 Settings + 局部覆盖”避免了到处传配置对象的样板；而把 Prompt 显式成模板，让 RAG 的“最后一公里语气与约束”可控可审。
“Global Settings + local overrides” kills the boilerplate of threading a config object everywhere; making the prompt an explicit template keeps RAG's “last-mile tone and constraints” controllable and auditable.

1. 新版 LlamaIndex 中，Settings 取代了什么？In recent LlamaIndex, what did Settings replace?

  2. ServiceContext（旧的全局配置）ServiceContext (the old global config)

答案：BAnswer: B Settings 是全局默认配置单例，取代了过去到处传递的 ServiceContext。Settings is the global default-config singleton that replaced the old, widely-passed ServiceContext.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 同样的检索结果，换一句 prompt 答案就不同。质量责任更多压在检索还是 prompt？你怎么分工调优、分别用什么指标？Same retrieved context, different prompt, different answer. Does quality rest more on retrieval or the prompt? How do you split the tuning, and with what metrics each?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：检索决定“依据对不对”、prompt 决定“依据用得对不对”——先把召回调达标，再用 prompt 调忠实度/格式。召回不到，prompt 再好也是巧妇难为无米之炊；指标上，检索看命中率/MRR，prompt 看 Faithfulness 与格式/约束达成率。别把两类问题混在一起调。🔑 Key: retrieval decides whether the evidence is right, the prompt decides whether it's used right — get recall to target first, then tune faithfulness/format with the prompt. No recall, no prompt can save it; measure retrieval by hit-rate/MRR and the prompt by Faithfulness plus format/constraint adherence. Don't conflate the two while tuning.
Prompt A（宽松）Prompt A (loose)
“根据资料回答” → 资料没提保修期，却补一句“一般为一年”(编造)。'answer from the context' → the warranty isn't there, yet it adds 'usually one year' (invented).
vs
Prompt B（严格）Prompt B (strict)
“只用资料、未提及就说不知道” → 老实回答“资料未提及”。'use only the context, say unknown otherwise' → honestly says 'not in the sources'.
检索一字不变，换 prompt 就改变忠实度——这是“最后一公里”Same retrieval, a different prompt changes faithfulness — the 'last mile'
🎯 2. 有人到处用全局 Settings、有人坚持显式传参。各自利弊？你怎么定团队规范？Some use the global Settings everywhere; others pass config explicitly. Trade-offs, and what team convention would you set?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：全局少样板但隐式依赖、难追踪、测试易串味；显式可读可测、可多配置共存但啰嗦。规范：全局设默认值，关键/差异化组件(评估用的 judge、特殊 query engine)显式覆盖并就近声明——既省样板又可追踪。🔑 Key: global means less boilerplate but an implicit, hard-to-trace dependency that can leak state in tests; explicit is readable/testable and lets configs coexist but is verbose. Convention: set sane global defaults, and explicitly override key/divergent components (an eval judge, a special query engine) declared close to use — boilerplate saved, traceability kept.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 同样的检索结果，换一句 prompt 就能改变答案——这把“质量责任”更多压在检索上还是 prompt 上？你怎么分工调优？Same retrieval, different prompt, different answer — does that put more of the quality burden on retrieval or on the prompt, and how would you split your tuning effort?
第四部分 · 进阶

18 · 进阶检索

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

基础 top-k 不够用时，进阶检索登场：融合多查询（QueryFusionRetriever）、自动合并相邻块（AutoMergingRetriever）、递归（RecursiveRetriever）、按问题路由到不同库（RouterRetriever）。它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever 接口。When plain top-k isn't enough, advanced retrieval steps in: fuse multiple queries (QueryFusionRetriever), merge adjacent chunks (AutoMergingRetriever), recurse (RecursiveRetriever), and route by question (RouterRetriever). All implement the same BaseRetriever interface.

一个问题One question
→
改写成多版Rephrase to N
LLM 生成 n-1 个LLM writes n-1 more
→
各自检索Retrieve each
每版取 top-ktop-k per variant
→
倒数排名融合Reciprocal rerank
跨多个排名累加summed across rankings
→
合并结果Merged set
去重后的统一列表one deduped list
Query Fusion：一题多问、分别检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合成一份结果Query Fusion: ask one question many ways, retrieve each, then reciprocal-rerank into a single result set
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
不只问一次、不只取一处：多角度改写再合并、把碎片拼回完整段落、按问题选对资料库。
Don't ask once or look in one place: rephrase from several angles and merge, stitch fragments back into a passage, and pick the right corpus per question.

基础 top-k 的三类短板，进阶检索逐一补齐Top-k's three weak spots — advanced retrieval patches each

把这些进阶检索当成一堆零散“高级技巧”去记，很容易迷失。换个视角：它们都在补朴素 top-k 相似度检索的三类典型短板——召回不全（换个问法本能命中的内容被漏掉）、命中碎片（块切得太碎，单个 Node 只剩半句上下文）、多库分流（不同问题其实该查不同索引）。看清这三道缺口，下面四种检索器就各有归属——其中“命中碎片”有横向合并、纵向递归两种补法；而且它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever，可即插即换、互相嵌套。
Memorizing advanced retrieval as a pile of scattered “tricks” gets you lost. Flip the view: they all patch plain top-k's three classic weak spots — missed recall (a different phrasing would have hit, but it's dropped), fragmented hits (chunks so small a single Node holds half a thought), and multiple corpora (different questions belong to different indexes). Name those three gaps and the four retrievers below each find their place — “fragmented hits” gets two cures, merging sideways and recursing down — and since all implement one BaseRetriever, you swap or nest them freely.
基础 top-k 的短板Top-k's weak spot
进阶检索器Advanced retriever
怎么补How it patches
召回不全Missed recall
QueryFusionRetrieverQueryFusionRetriever
一题多版改写再融合，覆盖更多说法multi-rephrase then fuse to cover more phrasings
命中碎片Fragmented hits
AutoMergingRetrieverAutoMergingRetriever
相邻子块自动合并回父块merge adjacent child chunks back into the parent
命中碎片Fragmented hits
RecursiveRetrieverRecursiveRetriever
从摘要/索引节点递归到完整原文recurse from summary/index nodes to the full source
多库分流Multiple corpora
RouterRetrieverRouterRetriever
由 LLM 选择该查哪个索引/工具an LLM picks which index/tool to query
三类短板组织起四种检索器：“命中碎片”有合并与递归两解，其余各对一招——接口统一，可单用也可叠加Three weak spots organize four retrievers: “fragmented hits” has two cures (merge, recurse), the rest map one-to-one — one interface, used alone or stacked

retrievers/fusion_retriever.py · QueryFusionRetriever — 多查询融合（含 reciprocal rerank）multi-query fusion (with reciprocal rerank)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
retrievers/auto_merging_retriever.py · AutoMergingRetriever — 相邻块自动合并auto-merging adjacent chunks
深入：融合检索与可插拔接口Deep dive: fusion retrieval and the pluggable interface点击展开expand
🧪 示例：一题改写成 4 版🧪 Example: rephrase one question into 4
QueryFusionRetriever(retrievers=[base], num_queries=4)：原问题加上 LLM 生成的 3 个改写各自检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合成一份去重结果，召回通常明显高于单版 top-k。
QueryFusionRetriever(retrievers=[base], num_queries=4): the original question plus 3 LLM-generated rewrites each retrieve, then reciprocal rerank fuses them into one deduped result set — recall usually beats single-query top-k by a clear margin.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
所有检索器都实现同一个 BaseRetriever，统一返回 list[NodeWithScore]，于是它们能互相嵌套、随意替换，并直接塞进任何 QueryEngine——上层完全无感。
Every retriever implements the same BaseRetriever and returns list[NodeWithScore], so they nest and swap freely and drop straight into any QueryEngine — the layer above never notices.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
num_queries=n 让 LLM 额外生成 n-1 个改写（原问题也算一版）；融合方式由 FUSION_MODES 决定，默认 simple，常显式设 reciprocal_rerank（RRF）——按每条结果在多个排名中的倒数位次累加打分，再统一排序。
num_queries=n makes the LLM generate n-1 extra rewrites (the original counts as one); fusion is governed by FUSION_MODES (default simple), and you commonly set reciprocal_rerank (RRF) — it sums each result's reciprocal rank across the several rankings, then sorts once.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
不是每个问题都靠“多问几遍”：碎片化严重就用 AutoMergingRetriever 合并回父块；知识有层级或引用就用 RecursiveRetriever 跟随引用到原文；面对多个索引就用 RouterRetriever 让 LLM 选库。它们可单用，也能叠在 fusion 之上。
Not every problem yields to “asking more times”: for heavy fragmentation use AutoMergingRetriever to merge back into parents; for hierarchical or cited knowledge use RecursiveRetriever to follow references to the source; for multiple indexes use RouterRetriever to let an LLM pick the corpus. Each works alone or stacked atop fusion.
进阶检索器仍是 BaseRetriever，可直接塞进 QueryEnginestill a BaseRetriever — drops into any QueryEngine
from llama_index.core.retrievers import QueryFusionRetriever

# 把一个问题改写成多版、分别检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合
fusion = QueryFusionRetriever(
    retrievers=[index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=5)],
    num_queries=4,
    mode='reciprocal_rerank',
)
nodes = fusion.retrieve('退款和换货政策有何不同？')
print(len(nodes))
另一种思路：AutoMerging 把命中的碎片拼回完整父块A different angle: AutoMerging stitches hit fragments back into a whole parent
from llama_index.core.retrievers import AutoMergingRetriever
from llama_index.core.node_parser import HierarchicalNodeParser

# 层级切块：同一段文本切成大/中/小三层父子块
parser = HierarchicalNodeParser.from_defaults()
nodes = parser.get_nodes_from_documents(docs)
# ...把叶子块建进 index，得到一个基础 base_retriever...
retriever = AutoMergingRetriever(
    base_retriever,                  # 任意 BaseRetriever（这里检索叶子块）
    storage_context=storage_context,
)
# 命中同一父块的多个叶子，会被自动合并成更完整的父块
merged = retriever.retrieve('保修条款有哪些例外情况？')
print(len(merged))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 进阶检索针对“召回不全/碎片化/多库”等基础 top-k 的短板。Advanced retrieval targets top-k's weak spots: missed recall, fragmentation, multiple corpora.
  • 它们都实现 BaseRetriever，可无缝接入现有 QueryEngine。All implement BaseRetriever, so they drop into an existing QueryEngine.
  • Fusion 用改写+融合提升召回；AutoMerging 用关系合并提升上下文完整度。Fusion lifts recall via rephrase+merge; AutoMerging lifts context completeness via relationships.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
进阶检索没有免费的午餐：fusion 多跑几轮检索来提召回，但更慢更贵；auto-merging 合并父块补上下文，却可能引入冗余。每一种都是在用更多计算换更好结果。
Advanced retrieval is no free lunch: fusion runs extra retrieval passes to lift recall but costs more and runs slower; auto-merging merges parent blocks to restore context but can add redundancy. Each trades more compute for better results.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 为什么进阶检索器能直接替换基础检索器、塞进原来的 QueryEngine？Why can advanced retrievers drop into an existing QueryEngine in place of the basic one?
  1. 因为它们更快Because they're faster
  2. 因为它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever 接口Because they all implement the same BaseRetriever interface
  3. 因为它们是 core 内置的Because they're built into core
  4. 因为它们不用 embeddingBecause they skip embeddings
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 统一的 BaseRetriever 接口让检索策略可插拔，QueryEngine 不感知具体实现。The uniform BaseRetriever interface makes retrieval strategies pluggable; the QueryEngine doesn't care which one.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 基础 top-k 召回不全。三类典型短板分别用哪种进阶检索器补？对延迟敏感的线上问答你会上 query fusion 吗？怎么权衡、怎么验证召回真提升？Naive top-k under-recalls. Which advanced retriever fixes each of the three typical weaknesses? Would you use query fusion in latency-sensitive live Q&A? How do you weigh it and verify recall actually improves?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：召回不全→Query Fusion、命中碎片→AutoMerging/Recursive、多库分流→Router；进阶检索是“用更多计算换更好结果”，没有免费午餐。延迟敏感时先量化：fusion 多跑几轮检索+一次改写，提升值不值这点延迟？高价值可容忍几百 ms 才上，否则用更便宜手段(更好 embedding/轻量 rerank/缓存)。验证：对 gold 集比较加 fusion 前后的命中率与端到端质量，再核延迟预算。🔑 Key: under-recall → Query Fusion, fragmented hits → AutoMerging/Recursive, multi-source → Router; advanced retrieval trades more compute for better results — no free lunch. Under latency pressure, quantify first: fusion adds retrieval passes + a rewrite — is the lift worth the latency? Adopt only for high-value, few-hundred-ms-tolerant flows; else use cheaper levers (better embedding/light rerank/caching). Verify by comparing hit-rate and end-to-end quality with/without fusion on a gold set, then re-check the latency budget.
